  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_afb1947f-1cb4-4340-8c47-0aa288c1d35e'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer3817403327777232110">To the outside world, they look like American Royalty, giving to charities, feeding the homeless, rebuilding the city. But behind closed doors is a constant battle for dominance between two Bosses, cultures, and hearts.<br/><br/><b>Ruthless People</b> is a romantic crime fiction set in modern day Chicago, following the life and marriage of Melody Nicci Giovanni and Liam Callahan—rivals by </span>
  <span id="freeText3817403327777232110" style="display:none">To the outside world, they look like American Royalty, giving to charities, feeding the homeless, rebuilding the city. But behind closed doors is a constant battle for dominance between two Bosses, cultures, and hearts.<br /><br /><b>Ruthless People</b> is a romantic crime fiction set in modern day Chicago, following the life and marriage of Melody Nicci Giovanni and Liam Callahan—rivals by blood and leaders through fear. Their marriage was arranged by their fathers in hopes to end years of bloodshed between the Irish and the Italians.<br /><br />Liam, next in line to lead the Irish, believes he’s getting a simple-minded wife, one he can control, one who bends to his every need . . . the complete opposite of Melody. Bred to be a Boss, a world-class marksman, master of disguise, with no mercy and no fear. Twenty-four years later, she has achieved more than any man could even dream of, killing anyone who steps in her way. She knows exactly what type of man Liam is, and she would rather die than give up the power she has spent her whole life building. But with no other family left, she must not only learn to work with Liam, but the whole Callahan clan.<br /><br />The Mafia of the past is evolving, and with rival bosses gunning for them, Melody and Liam will have to figure out how to work as one to take down those who stand in their way, all while keeping up appearances.<br /><br /><b>Power, Family, and Respect are everything.</b><br /><br /><i><b>Warning:</b> This book contains adult language and subject matter including graphic violence and explict sex that may be disturbing for some readers. This book is not intended for readers under the age of 18.</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13507829573062063742"><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/McAvoyRuthlesspeople1-3TitlebySueBee_zps47771bcc.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/RPstoryxBTbysb_zps79f18698.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400917150ra/9737574.gif' alt=' photo RPstoryxBTbysb_zps79f18698.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>★★★★★! Ruthless People, book 1 of 4. A whirlwind, blood-filled merger of two mafia houses and the power struggle / fuck-fest that ensues between a prodigal son & a mafia heiress!</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“She fucking shot me. I had been so shocked and horny that my mind couldn’t even comprehend what had happened.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/><u>Books in series should be read in order:</u><br/><b>Book 0.5: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1208945042' rel='nofollow noopener'>Declan + Coraline</a><br/>Book 1: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/899389201' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ruthless People</a><br/>Book 2: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/943295311' rel='nofollow noopener'>Untouchables</a><br/>Book 3: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/943324675' rel='nofollow noopener'>American Savages</a><br/>Book 4: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1477746746' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Bloody Kingdom</a></b><br/><br/><i>The <b>Ruthless People</b> t</i></span>
  <span id="freeText13507829573062063742" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/McAvoyRuthlesspeople1-3TitlebySueBee_zps47771bcc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400917150i/9737573.jpg" alt=" photo McAvoyRuthlesspeople1-3TitlebySueBee_zps47771bcc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/RPstoryxBTbysb_zps79f18698.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400917150ra/9737574.gif" alt=" photo RPstoryxBTbysb_zps79f18698.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★★! Ruthless People, book 1 of 4. A whirlwind, blood-filled merger of two mafia houses and the power struggle / fuck-fest that ensues between a prodigal son &amp; a mafia heiress!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“She fucking shot me. I had been so shocked and horny that my mind couldn’t even comprehend what had happened.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><u>Books in series should be read in order:</u><br><b>Book 0.5: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1208945042" rel="nofollow noopener">Declan + Coraline</a><br>Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/899389201" rel="nofollow noopener">Ruthless People</a><br>Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/943295311" rel="nofollow noopener">Untouchables</a><br>Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/943324675" rel="nofollow noopener">American Savages</a><br>Book 4: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1477746746" rel="nofollow noopener">A Bloody Kingdom</a></b><br><br><i>The <b>Ruthless People</b> trilogy follows <b>two mafia families</b>, <b>The Callahan’s</b> (Irish) and <b>The Giovanni’s</b> (Italian) in their merge, through marriage, with the intent of maintaining power, wealth and world domination through mainly drug trafficking and corruption by a.n.y. m.e.a.n.s. n.e.c.e.s.s.a.r.y.!</i><br><br><b>Ruthless People</b> (book 1) opens up to prodigal son <b>Liam Alec Callahan</b>, in bed with his mistress reflecting over the marriage contract that had been signed twelve years prior <b>between two of the most powerful mafia houses in the world</b> - his family and The Giovanni’s. <br><br>Liam has worked tirelessly alongside his father and the time has finally come for his father to <b>pass the reigns and title of Ceann na Conairte</b> to him. Heiress <b>Melody Nicci Giovanni</b> is the final piece in the puzzle. Through their marriage he will not only take over his father’s, but also her father’s mafia empire AND gain a meek wife to represent them to the world…<br><br>Nothing, I repeat nothing could have prepared Liam for Melody! For the past six years, in complete secrecy and hidden from the world, <b>Melody aka The Boss has been running her family empire</b> and she is not happy about her upcoming marriage. Needless to say their first meeting did not go well, mainly for Liam. LOL!<br><br>Story follows Liam and Melody, <b>America’s new favorite couple</b>, in the power struggle that ensues while Melody is integrated into her new family. What works in their favor is their <b>intense and undeniable sexual attraction</b>. They soon discover that they are extremely compatible in bed and based on that they can come to an understanding on how to run their empire.<br><br><b>Challenged for world domination</b> by The Valero’s (Russians) as well as the new Chicago Police Commissioner is quickly complicated by <b>set-backs</b> and more importantly when <b>feelings enter the picture</b>. Strap on your seatbelt for a ride like no other filled with <b>suspense, intrigue, murder, corruption, violence, manipulation</b> and… <b>mind-blowing sex!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“She looks like a sweet little lamb from afar, but when you get close, you find out she skinned and ate the damn thing just to use it as a coat. She’s a beast.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/RPhexBSbysb_zps4fe787ec.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400917150ra/9737575.gif" alt=" photo RPhexBSbysb_zps4fe787ec.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Melody Nicci Giovanni aka The Boss aka Bloody Melody</b> might go down in my book history! She had the perfect blend of strong, bad-ass heroine, vulnerable, broken girl and men-at-your-feet temptress with a temper! <br><br>Nine words to describe <b>Melody: V.o.l.a.t.i.l.e., motivated, competitive, fierce, smart, calculated, emotional, hot-headed and ruthless</b>.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“She is. . . she is Bloody Melody and perfect. God created her and then shattered the mold afterward, for the world could not handle two of her.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/RPHxBSbysb_zps686a708e.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400917150ra/9737576.gif" alt=" photo RPHxBSbysb_zps686a708e.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I don’t know who I love more <b>Liam Alec Callahan aka Ceann na Conairte</b> or his Melody. Much of my early enjoyment was derived from Liam’s fall into whopped, but he quickly landed on his feet and found a balance between <b>whopped, in charge and diplomacy</b>. As the layers are peeled, add to that the story about his childhood, and it’ll be hard not to <b>love this ruthless killer</b>.<br><br>Nine words to describe <b> Liam: Focused, cocky, calculated, reflective, jaded, hot-headed, vulnerable, diplomatic and ruthless</b>.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I loved being dominated in such a beastly sexual way. How his hands, lips and tongue all grabbed on to me.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><i>It takes <b>skill to write a story where the bad guys become the heroes &amp; the good guys are made into villains!</b> Just be warned, though I saw HUGE personal growth on both MCs and side characters, these people are savages with no remorse or compassion and their singular focus is selfish and superficial – within the confines of the family!</i><br><br><b>I devoured this story</b>; every page, every sentence, every word! The best way to describe the ending is the most <b>loose-ends were tied up</b> and we were given a <b>promising teaser</b> to the next chapter of their lives! I cannot wait for book 2, <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/943295311" rel="nofollow noopener">The Untouchables</a>
</b>.<br><br><b>Outstanding</b> character development! <b>Fascinating</b> heroine. <b>To-die-for</b> hero! <b>Brilliant</b> plot! <b>Mesmerizing</b> storytelling! <b>Hot-as-fuck</b> sex! This story reeks of 6-stars! My hat off to <b>J.J. McAvoy</b> for an <b>a.m.a.z.i.n.g. debut!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“That ticks me off!” She snapped. “Since when could you bribe me with treats like a fucking child.”<br>I groaned, pinching the bridge of my nose. “So no smoothie then?”<br>“Mango, banana, orange and extra kiwi,” she replied before hanging up.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 5+ stars <br>Heroine rating: 5+ stars<br>Sexual tension rating: 5+ stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 5+ stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 4.5 stars<br>Plot rating: 5 stars<br>Dialogue rating: 5+ stars<br>Storytelling rating: 5+ stars<br>Story ending rating: N/A<br>*********************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 5+ stars<br><br>Would I recommend this series: Yes, absolutely.<br>Would I re-read this series: Yes, absolutely.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/RPendxBbysb_zpsfdf2fc60.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400917150ra/9737577.gif" alt=" photo RPendxBbysb_zpsfdf2fc60.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Thanks to all my fellow buddy-readers on Shh…: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://goo.gl/En0XOU">https://goo.gl/En0XOU</a><br><br><b><i>ARC provided to me by author, J.J. McAvoy in exchange for an honest review.</i></b></i></span>

<div id="review_1549346096" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1549346096" />
    <a title="Lainey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22889537-lainey"><img alt="Lainey" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1391488417p2/22889537.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1549346096?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lainey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lainey" href="/user/show/22889537-lainey">Lainey</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22889537-lainey?shelf=did-not-finish">did-not-finish</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1549346096" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10370018826922089803">DNF @ 35%<br/>The Takeaway: Wikipedia is not a reliable source for research into organized crime. Neither is Google Translate for languages you clearly don't speak.<br/>The Takeaway #2: Mafias are not 007 James Bond spies. Stop acting like they are. <br/><br/>Well that was a huge swing and a miss.<br/><br/>I only got to about 35% before I honestly couldn't continue. And yet, I have more thoughts on this book than I do sometimes about books I actually completed. All I can really say about this book is: if you're going to do a</span>
  <span id="freeText10370018826922089803" style="display:none">DNF @ 35%<br />The Takeaway: Wikipedia is not a reliable source for research into organized crime. Neither is Google Translate for languages you clearly don't speak.<br />The Takeaway #2: Mafias are not 007 James Bond spies. Stop acting like they are. <br /><br />Well that was a huge swing and a miss.<br /><br />I only got to about 35% before I honestly couldn't continue. And yet, I have more thoughts on this book than I do sometimes about books I actually completed. All I can really say about this book is: if you're going to do a book about the mafia do your fucking research. I think some authors of this genre forget that while illegal, organized crime is a very real thing and inaccurately representing this lifestyle and culture to satisfy your own story's needs is a slap in the face. <br /><br />Synopsis: The Irish and the Italians decided awhile ago to marry off their kids to cement an alliance. Liam, from the Irish, is being prepped to take over his father's business and Melody is the only child of Orlando Giovanni - the Don of the Italians. (That's another thing, the term for the Italian head is Don not fucking Boss.) Little does anyone know that Orlando has been dying of cancer so Melody has been running her the ITALIAN FUCKING MAFIA SINCE SHE WAS 18. And trust me, I have more to say about that, I am just warming up. <br /><br />Ok, fuck, I have no idea where to start because I have so much boiling in me right now I need to center myself.<br /><br />Let's just get the characters over with. Melody. Jesus Christ. Quite honestly the worst female character I have ever read, and how the hell did she upset me having only read 35% of the book. People will argue that she's a strong, independent, temperamental, ruthless boss. NO. She is an immature, over-the-top, dramatic caricature. She is not even real. She's a psychopath. And trust me I LOVE psychopaths (enter Fredrik from the In The Company of Killers series by JA Redmerski) but what Melody lacked was her depth and humanity making her a very boring character, flat, and not even one-dimensional... whatever is less than that - that is what she was. <br /><br />Now excuse me because I just have to drag her right now. SHE IS TWENTY FOUR YEARS OLD. And she is Don of the Giovanni family. In what universe does the author think this is acceptable. I'm sick of seeing all these characters being so fucking young and running their crime groups. Honestly, you guys. There is a better chance that I, also at 24 years old, would become President of the United States. You see how impossible and insulting this is to the Mafia? I cannot. While it's not unheard of for women to have a place in the Mafia, it's not common. LEAST OF ALL TO BE THE DON. Give me a goddamn break. I liked the idea that she was behind-the-scenes for her dying father - that could have worked very well for the story. But head of the whole thing? Don't insult me. Not to mention there was no Consigliere in this book. The Italian mob can't run without one. The lack of knowledge of the Italian Mafia's hierarchy had my blood boiling. Any Wikipedia page I'm sure this author used as her sole research would have had a basic structure. Also, I wasn't a fan of how the Irish were portrayed either. The Irish Mob isn't as organized as it is in this book being portrayed like they are the Kardashians or some shit. No. They're not nearly as infamous as the Italians are. Not to mention their sole income is drugs? -sighs- Ok. Mafias always have their toes in multiple illegal activities. <br /><br />Now quick side note for females in organized crime: If you want to see a phenomenal portrayal of this, read Savages by Don Winslow and then do yourself a favor to see how Salma Hayek portrays it in the film because she alone makes that movie. She's also not 24 years old. <br /><br />Two more things Melody did that bothered THE FUCK out of me:<br />1. She intentionally kills a pregnant woman in the beginning. Ok. This would never happen coming from someone of the Italian Mob. They value woman and children and God so much this would never happen. The Cartel and the Triad is a different story. <br />2. She shoots up the Callahan's secret door because she's missing out on a meeting. A bullet hits the Irish crime boss in the chest - but thank fucking god he was wearing a bullet proof vest. This happens within the first 20% of the story and honestly, the story would have ended here because doing this WOULD HAVE GOTTEN HER KILLED because it was essentially seen as a hit on the boss. The Irish wouldn't have thought twice on shooting her. SHE WOULD HAVE BEEN DEAD. I AM SO ANGRY SHE WAS NOT SHOT FOR WHAT SHE DID.<br /><br />I'm still angry. I really have nothing to say about Liam except there was nothing remarkable about him, you could probably pick him up and drop him in some other mafia book - nothing about him stood out.<br /><br />Now let's talk about their relationship. Instalove. And laughable at that. I am all for the hate sex in books but literally the first time they have hate sex they decide they're gonna work together and rule the world and then at their wedding they're professing their undying devotion to each other. I can't. I honestly can't decide what is worse - the crime or the romance. <br /><br />I also saw really awkwardly worded sentences, incorrect grammar usage, and spelling mistakes. Also. I really want to talk about the language used in this. I am all for a well placed "fuck" in a sentence. But when I AM noticing how much cursing is in this book, I think you're overdoing it. Honestly. The curse words were a little excessive and didn't even drive the point home - they were kind of unnecessary. Again, if I'm saying that... <br /><br />I think that's all I have to say about the first 35% of the book. I feel marginally better ridding myself of this and getting my feelings off my chest. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10370018826922089803" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22735659-ruthless-people">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=5">5</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=alpha">alpha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=boss-n-billionaires">boss-n-billionaires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=bad-ass-chick">bad-ass-chick</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=darkerside-mindfuckery">darkerside-mindfuckery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=suspense-chills-n-thrills">suspense-chills-n-thrills</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer918533485" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10806505083529479295"><i>5 ruthlessly sexy stars</i><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I. Am. All. You. Have. Just as you are all I have – My family and loyalty start with you and you alone.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398832061i/9469825.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Two powerful families, two cultures, merged together to create one force, one rule. To the outside world they are royalty; elegant, classy, charitable and family oriented but to everyone else they are the Boss and the Ceann na Conairte. Apart they are your worst nightmare, but together they own you, mind, body and soul. <br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>He was known as the “Boogeyman o</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText10806505083529479295" style="display:none"><i>5 ruthlessly sexy stars</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I. Am. All. You. Have. Just as you are all I have – My family and loyalty start with you and you alone.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398832061i/9469825.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Two powerful families, two cultures, merged together to create one force, one rule. To the outside world they are royalty; elegant, classy, charitable and family oriented but to everyone else they are the Boss and the Ceann na Conairte. Apart they are your worst nightmare, but together they own you, mind, body and soul. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>He was known as the “Boogeyman of the East,” and I was the unknown “Wicked Witch of the West.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The rivalry between the Italians and the Irish has gone on long enough, coming to an end with the marriage of Liam and Melody. Honoring their father’s and family’s wishes, it is time for them to step up, take the reins and merge their forces to rule the world. It doesn’t matter that they have never met, what matters is how it benefits their family. <br><blockquote>
<b><i>Rule One:</i></b> You kill for family. You die for family. Because you can’t trust anyone else. <br><br><b>Rule Two:</b> Take no prisoners and have no regrets about it. <br><br><b>Rule Three:</b> Just because you sell drugs for a living isn’t an excuse not to dress well.<br><br><b>Rule Four:</b> No bloody divorce.</blockquote><br>Liam was under the impression he was going to get a mouse for a wife, someone who the world would fall in love with to cover their true line of business, but instead he got a cold hearted boss who is even more dangerous than he is because she looks like a mouse but has a heart of a lion. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398830284i/9469652.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A battle for dominance sets off and it’s up to them to come to a truce and compromise their demands for the good of the family...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Everything we don’t agree on, we fuck out.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398829000ra/9469485.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They come up with their own rules, ones that will ensure their future, their success and take the world by storm...<br><blockquote>
<b><i>Rule One:</i></b> After, or during, our meeting and chats we make sure to fuck each other’s brains out.<br><br><b>Rule Two:</b> We never use a condom<br><br><b>Rule Three:</b> We trust no one but each other.</blockquote><br>Melody considers this another business transaction, willing to commit herself to the family and her husband, but nothing more. The only thing between her and Liam is sex, no-holds-bar-downright-ruthless-sex. Liam wants more than just her body and her mind, he wants her heart and soul and if he has to play dirty to get it, then so be it...<br><blockquote>
<b><i>Step one,</i></b> smother her with love. <br><br><b>Step two,</b> take that love away. <br><br><b>Step three,</b> drag the raw emotions out of her kicking and screaming.</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398832780ra/9469945.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>While trying to bring the families together, they have to also deal with the city coming down on them and other families wanting to take their new force down. Staying strong and relying on each other is the only way to come out alive, fuck the consequences. <br><br>I absolutely freakin LOVED <b>Ruthless People</b>, it was highly entertaining with two strong willed dominant personalities battling it out to be the one on top. It was raw, gritty, and ruthless... I loved the balance between class and punishment, just because you sold drugs for a living of killed a person or two doesn’t mean you can dress well, exude class, give to the needy and respect family morals and culture. Melody was a complete bad ass, sexy and charming and eerily frightening. Liam was ever the alpha man, but he respected his wife’s abilities and as much as he wanted to lock her away and protect her, he let her be free and be the person she was meant to be. <br><br>It was completely different than anything I ever read, and I totally appreciated the fact that the drama didn't revolve around stupidity, lying or cheating. I honestly hope and pray that there is more to come because this is one story that I will never forget and will definitely re-read. Some may find it over the top, after all it is fiction, but if you can accept the story for what it is, then you will enjoy just as much. So if you are in a mood for a fast-action-packed read that is full of steam and power play this is the book for you. <br><br><i>ARC kindly provided by The Writer's Coffee Shop Publishing House, via NetGalley, in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br>***Quotes above are taken from the ARC version of the book and may differ upon publication. <br></span>

<div id="review_904705458" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/904705458" />
    <a title="Patrycja" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja"><img alt="Patrycja" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586460589p2/6852653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/904705458?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer904705458" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2981680811518963792"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b> Ruthless People<br/><b>Series:</b> Ruthless People #1<br/><b>Author:</b> JJ McAvoy<br/><b>Release Date: </b> July 17, 2014<br/><b>Rating:</b> 4 stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Not yet  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>They say that everything is black or white, good or bad, that there is no in between. Evil is just evil. And in ‘normal’, real life I would agree, but in places where the fiction rules, where we can tip toe around the edge and even dive into the world of VIOLENCE without the conscience, I am not seeing something as bad or good,</span>
  <span id="freeText2981680811518963792" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b> Ruthless People<br><b>Series:</b> Ruthless People #1<br><b>Author:</b> JJ McAvoy<br><b>Release Date: </b> July 17, 2014<br><b>Rating:</b> 4 stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Not yet  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They say that everything is black or white, good or bad, that there is no in between. Evil is just evil. And in ‘normal’, real life I would agree, but in places where the fiction rules, where we can tip toe around the edge and even dive into the world of VIOLENCE without the conscience, I am not seeing something as bad or good, I’m only seeing it in fun category. And Ruthless People not only delivered no stopping entertainment,<b> it totally knocked me on my ass. </b><br><br>You have to know, I’m the good type of girl – polite (usually), respectful, hard-working, the usual ‘normal’ law abiding citizen. I’ve never stolen anything or hurt anyone, I have never even got a speeding ticket, and while I feel disgusted by those who break law on normal basis, I definitely can make exception for fictional mafia family, J.J McAvoy created. <b>The Callahan’s were the bomb!</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397321229i/9262847.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>You kill for family. You die for family. Because you can’t trust anyone else.</i>
</b><br><br>The gore, the blood, the suspense, the animalistic bloodlust… <br> <br>Ruthless People have it all. This novel is definitely not dark read, it is so much more. The characters are not good people, their hearts are not made of gold, nor will that change. It’s not a story of people who don’t have a choice, it’s a tale of complete surrender to your dark demons. It’s a book about feeling good while doing bad. <br><br>From the very first page reader is thrown into the world without scruples. There is no time to slowly sink into a poodle of it and then go deeper to gently let go of morals. In a matter of seconds we learn the gruesome rules of Mafia, that won’t change. They are not pleasant, nor fair. They are simply horrible. But the Callahan’s and Giovanni’s breathe them in. They live by them. And Liam Callahan and Melody Giovanni crave them. They need them to function.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397321229i/9262848.jpg" width="400" height="600" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As the future heads of the Irish and Italian mafia, Liam and Mel know they have to show the other who’s the boss; They feel the need to rule the world and make those against them bleed. The two completely stubborn, merciless and blood craving villains are counting days till they meet each other in the altar to connect family’s businesses and finally become the boss. But the thing is the leader can be only one, but nor Mel nor Liam are ready to give it up. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397321229i/9262849.jpg" width="400" height="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In a strange mix of lust, blood and constant fight for the position, both of them are getting closer to become the true wife and husband or to stabbing the other one in sleep. <br><br><b>Who will win? The merciless, arrogant and deadly Liam or the dangerous, lethal and complete bitch Melody?</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397321505i/9262871.jpg" width="400" height="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I still feel pretty exhausted. Ruthless People is definitely demanding read. It not only challenges reader by the fast pace and extreme plot, it sucks her right into the deep hole. You know it’s bad to feel so high and good while reading about such things, but you just can’t help yourself. Every blood covered page is a new dare. <br><br>You have to be warned that there is no GOOD there. There is only crime, misconduct and corruption and lots of lots of sex. The characters are Villains with big V. And that won’t change. Mel was and will be a bitch. She will kill the innocents just because she feels like it. She will shoot right between the eyes and won’t even feel a pang of guilt. Liam will kill only to feel the pleasure… Together they are crazy.<br><br>This is not a book for everyone, so keep that in mind but, If you are a fan of Dexter, Sons of Anarchy, Sopranos or other villains you will definitely enjoy Ruthless People. It will knock your socks off. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I want you to be willing to kill for me. I want you to be the same killer I am and not flinch away from the blood. I want you to revel in the blood alongside me. I want you to help me take down every fucker who stands in the way of a Callahan.”</i>
</b><br><br><br>JJ McAvoy focused very much on mafia and what it means to be bad, but the romance between the Mel and Liam was still incredibly hot and heavy. The banter (if I can call it that) between them was extremely over the top in the best meaning of this word. It was so intense to watch them fight and beat each other senseless only to see them end up having the hottest sex ever. <br><br><b>Why not the five stars then? </b><br><br>There were two things that irritated me. Firstly, I wished love/hate between Liam and Mel lasted a little longer. Few days was definitely not enough time for them to get along well, and I missed them fighting. Secondly, the story had few alternating point of views. I was tired of being interrupted by other characters and what they were saying. The story’s progress wouldn’t change at all without it. <br><br><b>But despite that, Ruthless people is kick ass start to absolutely powerful series, I will definitely be following. </b><br><br><br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON: <b><br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Twitter"         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer960910305" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4446763220486099572"><b>Live now on Amazon!!!! <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.amazon.com/Ruthless-People-J-J-McAvoy-ebook/dp/B00LVA6QYM/ref=sr_1_2?ie=UTF8&qid=1405601396&sr=8-2&keywords=ruthless+people+kindle'>http://www.amazon.com/Ruthless-People...</a> </b><br/><br/>I must begin this review by thanking J.J. McAvoy. You have written an amazing book, and I feel like it was written just for me! <i>Sorry, everyone else, but this baby is mine…</i> <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380905371ra/3150879.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Ruthless People is sexy, witty, and suspenseful. Every time I put it down I had mixed feelings. You know when you <b>love</b> a book so much on one hand you think I have to finish this, but self preservation kicks in and you think if I take my time I can enjoy it longer</span>
  <span id="freeText4446763220486099572" style="display:none"><b>Live now on Amazon!!!! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Ruthless-People-J-J-McAvoy-ebook/dp/B00LVA6QYM/ref=sr_1_2?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1405601396&amp;sr=8-2&amp;keywords=ruthless+people+kindle">http://www.amazon.com/Ruthless-People...</a> </b><br><br>I must begin this review by thanking J.J. McAvoy. You have written an amazing book, and I feel like it was written just for me! <i>Sorry, everyone else, but this baby is mine…</i> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380905371ra/3150879.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Ruthless People is sexy, witty, and suspenseful. Every time I put it down I had mixed feelings. You know when you <b>love</b> a book so much on one hand you think I have to finish this, but self preservation kicks in and you think if I take my time I can enjoy it longer. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402443087ra/9937939.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Okay, well I stayed up until 3:30 am last night, because I have no self control. So what if I am little less productive/awake at work today. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402443087ra/9937940.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Enough about me lets talk about these <i>Ruthless People</i>. <br><br><b>Liam Alec Callahan</b> is cocky, arrogant, controlling, manipulative, hothead and attractive. In other words, Liam is my freaking favorite type of alpha male. <br><br><b>Melody Nicci Giovanni</b> is beautiful, deadly, stunning, and the Boss. <br><br>With their marriage they are going to join the East and the West, the Italians and Irish. However, both are used to being in charge and calling the shots. Together these two have to learn how to rule an army together, oh and live together as husband and wife. <br><br>These two are as <i>ruthless</i> as it comes. There is no limit to how far they will go to be successful. While some would say reading about murder and death would make this a dark read, there was enough humor to lighten it up. The combination of sexiness, humor, and darkness is a perfect balance. <br><br>I have thought about this book all day, and I stand by my earlier statement <b>my favorite book so far this year.</b><br><br>Should you read this book...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402443087ra/9937941.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC provided to me by author, J.J. McAvoy in exchange for an honest review.</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="4446763220486099572" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_971066612" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/971066612" />
    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/971066612?book_show_action=true">Jun 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781612133201" href="/book/show/22237407-ruthless-people">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-heroine">favorite-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-alpha-hero">favorite-alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=fav-new-author">fav-new-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=faves">faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=books-with-an-edge">books-with-an-edge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=dark-read">dark-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=kick-ass-heroine">kick-ass-heroine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer971066612" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13146252038804720702"><b>4.5 Ruthlessly Delicious Stars</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403205860i/10058297._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>She would never convert to what I needed her to be. She was a ruthless savage, and if you cannot break a ruthless savage, you need to figure out how to tame them.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398396764ra/9409745.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>When the first line in the book blurb is this:<br/><blockquote>
  <b>"Mr. & Mrs. Smith meets the Sopranos..."</b>
</blockquote><br/>A bitch can get wary. I mean, it can't possibly be THAT delicious of a combination, right? No way will it live up to my expectations of gritty, erotic, amazing banter, with mafia savages that you can't help</span>
  <span id="freeText13146252038804720702" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Ruthlessly Delicious Stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403205860i/10058297._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">She would never convert to what I needed her to be. She was a ruthless savage, and if you cannot break a ruthless savage, you need to figure out how to tame them.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398396764ra/9409745.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>When the first line in the book blurb is this:<br><blockquote>
  <b>"Mr. &amp; Mrs. Smith meets the Sopranos..."</b>
</blockquote><br>A bitch can get wary. I mean, it can't possibly be THAT delicious of a combination, right? No way will it live up to my expectations of gritty, erotic, amazing banter, with mafia savages that you can't help but love to hate...and just simply love. Right? RIGHT?! <b>WRONG</b>. Because it really was that perfect combination and so much more. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>Rule One: You kill for family. You die for family. Because you can't trust anyone else</b>
</blockquote><br>If you're looking for a book with a heroine that's almost more ruthless and bloodthirsty than the Irish mob hero, and an all around bad bitch, look no further. Meet Melody Giovanni <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403287459i/10071335._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The daughter of the biggest Italian mafia boss in Chicago, and soon to be wife of Liam Callahan. Their marriage, arranged by their fathers in hopes to end years of bloodshed between the Irish and the Italians, is also bound to combine two of the biggest mafia families. Too bad Mel is not exactly the docile little mafia princess that Liam has been expecting<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397424132ra/9273955.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">...do not ever put your fucking lips on me without my permission."<br>"My mother told me never to hit a woman, but you are pushing my limits."<br>"Funny, my father told me the same thing. Would you like me to apologize?"<br>"Third, if you ever interrupt me again, Liam Alec Callahan, may God have mercy on your soul when I send you to meet him."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The banter between these two was one of my favorite parts of this book. Mel is one cold and ruthless bitch. This is definitely not a book for everybody. But I gobbled it up like a starving junky.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Say you're sorry and I will free you now, love, and then we can start anew"<br>He was trying to break me, the fucker.<br>"Fuck you and the Audi you drove up in."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403287737ra/10071378.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This is no ordinary power couple. The things that both of them do is certainly not for the faint of heart. But hey, you're reading about the 2 heads of powerful mafia families. You didn't expect kittens and rainbows, did you?<br><blockquote>
  <b>Rule Two: Take no prisoners and have no regrets about it.</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387222702ra/7553867.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I was sucked into the story from the first chapter. The action, the banter, the characters. Everything about this book worked for me. Did I also mention the banter?<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Declan leaned into me. "When she wakes up in the morning, the devil curses."<br>"We both do," I muttered.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403289025i/10071591._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>Rule Three: Just because you sell drugs for a living isn't an excuse not to dress well.</b>
</blockquote><br>A couple that tortures together, stays together. And the fact that they're both gorgeous and burn up the sheets with some of the best angry sex you'll ever read? Icing on the murder cake.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403289615i/10071713._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>Rule Four: No bloody divorce.</b>
</blockquote><br>But with a ruthless powerhouse couple like these two, why would you even think that?<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Fucking Jesus, Liam."<br>"Not even he can save you from this now."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403289615ra/10071714.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Quick paced, action packed, erotic, gritty, and addicting as fuck. There is a cliffhanger, but it wasn't as bad as most you'll find in books now. It ended in a satisfying enough way that even my cliffhanger avoiding ass didn't end up in a tizzy. <br><br><b>Writing Style</b> First person POV (Dual, with a few instances of other POV's thrown in). I actually really enjoyed the additional POVs. Typically I'd find something like that confusing, but I really felt it added to the story in this case.<br><br><i>ARC courtesy of publisher via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><b>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436206i/881587.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="13146252038804720702" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_899616305" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/899616305" />
    <a title="Lucia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia"><img alt="Lucia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484242793p2/8837962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/899616305?book_show_action=true">Apr 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer899616305" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7192147016808515819">My Liam and Melody:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405533388i/10411454._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>3.5 STARS<br/><br/>What a ride! I love when I come across something original and refreshing. And this book is exactly that.</b><br/><br/><i>Liam, 27-years old "soon-to-be head of the irish Mob" is about to marry Melody, 24-years old heir of Italian Mafia in arranged marriage. Liam thinks that his wife will be putty in his hands as soon as he puts his charms into the use. But he is in for a rude awakening because Melody is like nothing Liam expected. And so starts not so lovely love story between Liam Ca</i></span>
  <span id="freeText7192147016808515819" style="display:none">My Liam and Melody:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405533388i/10411454._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>3.5 STARS<br><br>What a ride! I love when I come across something original and refreshing. And this book is exactly that.</b><br><br><i>Liam, 27-years old "soon-to-be head of the irish Mob" is about to marry Melody, 24-years old heir of Italian Mafia in arranged marriage. Liam thinks that his wife will be putty in his hands as soon as he puts his charms into the use. But he is in for a rude awakening because Melody is like nothing Liam expected. And so starts not so lovely love story between Liam Callahan and Melody Giovanni...</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405533388i/10411455._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>RUTHLESS.</b> As title itself indicates; storyline, events and characters in this novel are ruthless. But I wasn't expecting anything else. Afterall, this is a novel about two most powerful mafia families. So don't go into this book expecting fairytale or other terribly romantic story, you aren't going to find it here. But what you are going to get, is one explosive, intense and sexy thriller!<br><br><b>LETHAL.</b> That's exactly the best word to describe main protagonists. Both Liam and Melody have no remorse about the kind of work they do. They were born with killing and violence in their veins and that's how they have always lived. Would they be a perfect match or a deadly coctail for each other?<br><br><b>COLD-BLOODED.</b> Melody is like none female heroine I have ever read about. As a first female Boss of mafia, she has to be extra bloody and power-hungry. I really liked that Melody stays true to her character through out the whole story and author never tried to unrealistically change her. Plus I liked the crazy dynamics between all main protagonists. It was such a fun to read about!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405533388i/10411456._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Do not hesitate to pick this book up so you can meet possessive and hot-headed Irish mob king; his ruthless and rough Italian queen; as well as their families.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405533388i/10411457._SY540_.jpg" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><i>*ARC provided by publisher as an exchange for honest review*</i><br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>
</a><br></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=so-happy-i-read-this">so-happy-i-read-this</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1214736728" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9898125089481230254">|4.5 gotta get me some Irish and Italian stars|<br/><br/>￼<br/><br/>Rules:<br/><br/>*You kill for family. You die for family. Because you can't trust anyone else.<br/>*Take no prisoners and have no regrets about it.<br/>*Just because you sell drugs for a living isn't an excuse not to dress well.<br/>*No bloody divorce.<br/>*Never displease your mother.<br/><br/><br/>Blurb: To the outside world, they look like American Royalty, giving to charities, feeding the homeless, rebuilding the city. But behind closed doors is a constant battle for dominance between two</span>
  <span id="freeText9898125089481230254" style="display:none">|4.5 gotta get me some Irish and Italian stars|<br /><br />￼<br /><br />Rules:<br /><br />*You kill for family. You die for family. Because you can't trust anyone else.<br />*Take no prisoners and have no regrets about it.<br />*Just because you sell drugs for a living isn't an excuse not to dress well.<br />*No bloody divorce.<br />*Never displease your mother.<br /><br /><br />Blurb: To the outside world, they look like American Royalty, giving to charities, feeding the homeless, rebuilding the city. But behind closed doors is a constant battle for dominance between two Bosses, cultures, and hearts.<br />Ruthless People is a romantic crime fiction set in modern day Chicago, following the life and marriage of Melody Nicci Giovanni and Liam Callahan—rivals by blood and leaders through fear. Their marriage was arranged by their fathers in hopes to end years of bloodshed between the Irish and the Italians.<br />Liam, next in line to lead the Irish, believes he’s getting a simple-minded wife, one he can control, one who bends to his every need... the complete opposite of Melody. Bred to be a Boss, a world-class marksman, master of disguise, with no mercy and no fear. Twenty-four years later, she has achieved more than any man could even dream of, killing anyone who steps in her way. She knows exactly what type of man Liam is, and she would rather die than give up the power she has spent her whole life building. But with no other family left, she must not only learn to work with Liam, but the whole Callahan clan.<br />The Mafia of the past is evolving, and with rival bosses gunning for them, Melody and Liam will have to figure out how to work as one to take down those who stand in their way, all while keeping up appearances.<br /><br />Power, Family, and Respect are everything.<br /><br />￼<br /><br />To say that I’ve been meaning to read this book since it came out it’d be nothing but the truth.<br />I’ve seen a lot of people loving it but I still wasn’t sure if that was going to be my case. Too many expectations, you know? But holy moly I absolutely loved Mel and Liam’s story and their world.<br /><br />It was only chapter one and I was already in love. I loved how violent it was and sophisticated and sexy and dark and funny. I enjoyed McAvoy’s storytelling and how her characters grew in the story, it was really great.<br /><br />Let’s talk about Liam fucking Callahan, thank you.<br /><br />That guy was absolutely amazing. He was smart, hot, dedicated, ruthless, funny, charming and evil. I loved him oh so much since the beginning and arg! How can I describe this man? Like really describe him? I cannot because if I start like really thinking about him, I’m going to start giggling like a 5 years old and wouldn’t be able to continue typing.<br />Damn, he was such a strong character and I loved how his mindset changed the instant he met Mel. He wanted this preppy, docile wife and when he found this beautiful and bloody woman, he wanted her that way. He’s the king and as such he’s going rule along Mel with iron fist. <br /><br />Get it?<br /><br />￼<br /><br />Yeah, so I also really loved how invested in the marriage he was from the start and how he planned getting Mel to fall for him. Plus, is it odd I found incredible hot how he killed people and how he plotted world domination? What can I say, I love power and Liam’s a man who knows exactly what he wants and how to get it.<br /><br />￼<br /><br />Now, Melody. Ah, my Bloody Melody…<br />I did not expect for me to love her this much, truly. I thought I was just going to like her but nope, I was in love with her since the very moment she threated that guy in her private jet.<br />She is so motherfucking amazing, that woman made my motherfucking week. <br />She was classy, deadly, beautiful, skilled, smart, ruthless, cunning… I mean, she is the Boss. Gods, I have such a crush on her. Like wow.<br /><br />Thing is, I found myself being more in love with her in those moments when you wouldn’t believe she could do harm. Like, when she was in bed with Liam and he said something she didn’t like and the she just pulled a knife out? Those moments were so cool, I don’t know what to tell you, I’m amazed by her in any possible way.<br /><br />I loved her character the most, I won’t lie. I loved how she evolved in the story, how she let some things go and how she never stopped being who she was. All the struggles she went through, before and after meeting Liam, made her this incredible woman. <br />I have no words for her, she was the fucking star.<br /><br />￼<br /><br />Here, I made a poem just for them:<br /><br /><br /><br />Roses are red<br />Violets are blue<br />She’s so hot, god<br />I wanna like her up<br />See the moon<br />See the sun<br />I wanna fuck that man<br />Till I have his son<br /><br /><br /><br />I mean, they're bloody hot together.<br /><br />￼<br /><br />As for the rest of the characters, I really enjoyed reading about them and getting to know them a bit more.<br />I actually liked it a lot. I didn’t expect to like Olivia but at the end of the day, I did like her and I loved reading about their relationships. It was pretty cool knowing they all love each other and how loyal they are.<br /><br />Overall I absolutely loved this story and I’d like to reread it in the near future. I also loved the quotes at the beginning of each chapter. They were rather fitting and that damned ending, omg. I did not see that coming, honestly.<br /><br />Guys, go read this book and love it with me, please.<br /><br />￼</span>
  <a data-text-id="9898125089481230254" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11948992755004078855"><b>4 Batshit Crazy Stars</b><br/><br/>This is going to be a short and quick review not worthy of this book, but I'm just not in a review mood at the moment. <br/><br/>This was <i>crazy</i> awesome in that the characters were (as I said in my review title, just to be redundant) <b>bat shit crazy</b>. <br/><br/>Seriously. <br/><br/>Melody and Liam were fucking nuts. <br/><br/>They say that psychopathy is a creation of nature (you are born that way) and sociopathy is a result of <s>jacked the fuck up</s> nurturing or environment. Now, obviously I am not an expert and I'm ove</span>
  <span id="freeText11948992755004078855" style="display:none"><b>4 Batshit Crazy Stars</b><br><br>This is going to be a short and quick review not worthy of this book, but I'm just not in a review mood at the moment. <br><br>This was <i>crazy</i> awesome in that the characters were (as I said in my review title, just to be redundant) <b>bat shit crazy</b>. <br><br>Seriously. <br><br>Melody and Liam were fucking nuts. <br><br>They say that psychopathy is a creation of nature (you are born that way) and sociopathy is a result of <s>jacked the fuck up</s> nurturing or environment. Now, obviously I am not an expert and I'm oversimplifying something way serious...however, Liam and Melody have...issues.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406557097ra/10565544.gif" width="500" height="211" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>They are awful people who do awful things. They commit every heinous crime under the sun and they have no qualms or remorse about any of it. <br><br><b>But I <i>loved</i> them for it.</b><br><br>Because this was a book about the damned Mafia, folks, and the Mafia doesn't fuck around. <br><br>So many times authors write books about gangs or motorcycle clubs, but they sugarcoat what they do or make them into reformed criminals who were either regretful of their crimes or doing it under the guise of making something right (I'm looking at you my beloved Kristen Ashley). <br><br>But nay nay, not J.J.McAvoy. She totally went balls to the wall on this and made her Mafia the damned <i>Mafia</i> people. <br><br>LOVE it. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406557677ra/10565584.gif" width="500" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>My ONLY complaint with this story was the time frame. I felt that certain things moved waaaaaay too fast. <br><br>For example, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[nine days after meeting each other, Liam is expecting Melody's trust and undying devotion and they are oh so in love? <br><br>These are two people who have been raised in Mafia families and trained to hate each other since birth and distrust <i>everyone</i>, even family members. <br><br>So I have a hard time swallowing how fast they moved. I feel like their progression should have spanned over the course of months (at <i>least</i>) not days.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>But maybe that's just me. <br><br>Otherwise, this book was great and I can't wait for #2 and more from McAvoy in general. </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1287969338?book_show_action=true">May 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22735659-ruthless-people">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dangerous-hero-themed-books-read">dangerous-hero-themed-books-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dark-themes">dark-themes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=hate-that-i-love-them">hate-that-i-love-them</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=pregnant-heroines">pregnant-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1287969338" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3928047419045367670"><strong>Ruthless Is Putting It Mildly.</strong><br/><br/>Liam and Melody are anything but a conventional couple. Pushed together in an arranged marriage in order to merge two large mafia families, it is a battle of wills right from the start. Halfway through this book I still wasn't sure if they were going to end up killing each other!<br/><br/>Liam is the sexy, hot-headed and greatly feared next-in-line head of the Irish mob in Chicago. He is known for his icy demeanor and take-no-prisoners attitude. He is a force to be reckoned w</span>
  <span id="freeText3928047419045367670" style="display:none"><strong>Ruthless Is Putting It Mildly.</strong><br /><br />Liam and Melody are anything but a conventional couple. Pushed together in an arranged marriage in order to merge two large mafia families, it is a battle of wills right from the start. Halfway through this book I still wasn't sure if they were going to end up killing each other!<br /><br />Liam is the sexy, hot-headed and greatly feared next-in-line head of the Irish mob in Chicago. He is known for his icy demeanor and take-no-prisoners attitude. He is a force to be reckoned with and this wedding will secure his position of dominance in the criminal hierarchy.<br /><br />Melody is a virtual unknown. However, the extent of her mafia dealings is soon revealed. She is no wallflower. She is more cutthroat than the toughest of the men she's commanded as the behind the scenes Boss for the past several years. She has proven herself time and time again, rising to the top of the mafia hierarchy and earning the respect of her men.<br /><br />Liam expects a wife that will decorate his arm at charity galas and otherwise, remain conveniently unaware of his criminal dealings. Melody has no intention of giving up an ounce of the power that she fought tooth and nail to attain. As these two try to come to terms with what married life means for them, blood will be shed and nobody will walk away unscathed.<br /><br />This is not a sweet and heart-warming type of love story. If you're looking for grand romantic gestures, roses and candlelit dinners, you won't find it here. The love is gradual and grows from passionate and antagonistic roots. This couple offers no apologies and begs for no ones forgiveness.<br /><br />I really liked this story and will be continuing the series. It was quite different than other mafia-themed romances and I loved the fact that Melody was such a badass. <br /><br />I went back and forth over whether to give this one 3 or 4 stars, only because there were so many grammatical errors. Ultimately, I decided that the story was compelling enough that it warranted 4 stars. Hopefully, additional editing will be done for any future editions.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3928047419045367670" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer950945391" class="readable"
              >

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>
