        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1060692467" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12152374148038644570"><b>
  <i>4***Bloody Mel Stars</i>
</b><br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=30aqbz6' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431915213ra/14882466.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><p>
  <b>
    <i>“She was mine. She was all fucking mine….I was the king of the jungle, and the woman beside me was my queen.” Leam</i>
  </b>
</p><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=1677b7n' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431915213i/14882467._SY540_.jpg' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This story takes place in the city of Chicago. Were three families stronger than all the rest in the mafia world are fighting to take control of their city. The Callahan, the Giovanni, and the Valero. <br/> <br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=vsns4y' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431915213ra/14882468.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>Leam Alex Callahan</b> was a cocky, gorgeous twenty seven year old man. His family had arranged his marriage when he was young with the Giov</span>
  <span id="freeText12152374148038644570" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>4***Bloody Mel Stars</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=30aqbz6" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431915213ra/14882466.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><p>
  <b>
    <i>“She was mine. She was all fucking mine….I was the king of the jungle, and the woman beside me was my queen.” Leam</i>
  </b>
</p><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=1677b7n" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431915213i/14882467._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This story takes place in the city of Chicago. Were three families stronger than all the rest in the mafia world are fighting to take control of their city. The Callahan, the Giovanni, and the Valero. <br> <br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=vsns4y" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431915213ra/14882468.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Leam Alex Callahan</b> was a cocky, gorgeous twenty seven year old man. His family had arranged his marriage when he was young with the Giovanni’s only daughter. The Callahan’s ruled Chicago and when they combined two of the most powerful families they were going to be unstoppable. Liam had green eyes, dark brown sex hair and a charming smile that melt every girl panties. His family was Irish and they could drink every day from dusk until dawn and still walk a straight line . Many feared Leam because he made himself well known. He was ruthless and cold blooded killer and wanted to earn the title his father was giving him. He was going to take over his father’s position once he marries. He was known as the “boogeyman of the east” because he was heart less and didn’t care what he had to do to get what he wanted. He had never met his “to be bride” before and he was not worried about it, just maybe a little bit but he just assumed she will be the shopping kind of girl that will stay at home. <br> <br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2j5dves" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431915213ra/14882469.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><u><b><i>“Rule One: You kill for family. You die for family. Because you can’t trust anyone.” </i></b></u><br><br><u><b><i>“Rule Two: Take no prisoners and have no regrets about it.” </i></b></u><br><br><u><b><i>“Rule Three: Just because you sell drugs for a living isn’t an excuse not to dress well.” </i></b></u><br><br><u><b><i>“Rule Four: No bloody divorce.”</i></b></u><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=x4lxms" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431915213i/14882470._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br><b>Melody Nicci Giovanni</b> was the only daughter of the Giovanni’s family. They were the most powerful family in Italy in the mafia world. She was the unknown “wicked witch of the west” but her man nicked named her “Bloody Melody” they all feared her. The world didn’t know she had stepped up and taken over her father’s empire. Her father was Ill with cancer and was going to die soon. He wanted to make sure she was married before that happened so they rushed the wedding. She was ruthless and savage and had been training since early age. She knew how to play the game and no one even thought what she was until they were put in front of her. She was twenty four years old with wavy black hair, flawless olive skin, deep brown eyes, and a bad as body to kill for. All the man drooled and lusted over her. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=eaiip2" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431915213ra/14882471.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><p><b><i>“You, ma’am, are ruthless, and not a soul on this planet would dare cross you. You would put a bullet in our heads if we were ever disloyal to you or the family. You are the Boss,” Reply one of her man</i></b></p><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=xby0d4" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431915213i/14882472._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><b>Leam and Melody</b> met each other just few days before their wedding. It was super hot because they fought like savage animals. At first he thought she was an ugly duck and when he saw her he knew he wanted her. He thought he could rule and controlled her but he was so damn wrong. She fought him as he stopped her killing and they had a ruthless kissing scene but he ended up with a shot on his leg, and both ended up with bruises, it was awesome really haha. They had to go to battle before the wedding and they ended up hooking up, like Damn! it was freaking hot. They got married and their sex was even hotter every single time. At first it was lust that they found on each other however the more time spent together the more they realized they are both lonely and they have been searching for someone like them the entire time. It was like they were both just meant to be because they both has no remorse of what they did for living and were ruthless that did not hesitate to kill whoever gets on their way. They both have found their perfect match. It was Leam who had to teach Mel how to love because she honestly had never felt love before so she was struggling, he handled her amazingly. Prompts to him to put up with her bossiness but again they were just both made perfectly for each other, I absolutely loved these two.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=iyoqk4" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431915213ra/14882473.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2hzz91" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431915213ra/14882474.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><p><b><i>“You stand at my side. I stand at yours, and together we rule the East and the West, so much so that they’ll rename cities after us.” Leam</i></b></p><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2954ncp" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431915213ra/14882475.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><p><b><i> “May we be ruthless and have no regrets…May we take what we want, when we want it, with the world at out feet.” Mel</i></b></p><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=o5rqki" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431915213ra/14882476.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>There was so much action and suspense going on through this story. A lot of deaths, fights, and the entire city were in chaos. People were dying front and right because the police was trying to catch The Callahan’s family and lock them down on top of that the Valero’s family was after them too. So the war was real. This book kept me on the edge constantly not knowing what was coming up next. There were so many surprises and secrets and I was speechless by the time I was done. The author was able to get you to love the entire Callahan family.<br> <br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=zn0do9" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431915213ra/14882477.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2uo2dmd" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431915213ra/14882478.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=25zge4k" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431915213ra/14882479.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mc8zea" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431915213ra/14882480.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>The story was told in Leam and Melody’s POVs however, we got multiple POVs from the family members, not much but I really enjoyed knowing a little bit more about them. After reading Declan (Leam’s cousin) and his wife Cora’s thoughts, I felt more understandable to what they were going thru. Also his brother Neal and wife Olivia, now they really touched me and I really wish they had their own book because I couldn't help hurting for them. Leam’s parents were awesome; I enjoyed learning about them a little more thru the father’s POV. We also get to know Mel’s private pro-filer Adriana; her story was crazy she was a total bad ass. I really liked her a lot and after reading what she went through and how Mel helped her out I had so much more respect for them both. I felt so attached to all these characters at the end of the book that I just can’t get enough. I will most defiantly be continuing this series. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2j4uid1" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431915213ra/14882481.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><p><b><i> “The Family that mourns together survives forever.” J.J. McAvoy</i></b></p><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=30i9b4m" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431322182ra/14824299.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br><i>BR In Honor of our Friend</i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/30466081-sasha-elle-a-k-a-mrs-liam-callahan" rel="nofollow noopener">Sasha Elle</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/2362349-toppicks-with-alessandra-suebee-may-10-sasha-elle-week-ruthless-p?ref=ru_lihp_cm_tp_1_mclk-up2339441405#comment_id_119035415" rel="nofollow noopener">Shh</a><br><br><br><b><i>Book series order:</i><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21839603.Ruthless_People__Ruthless_People___1_" title="Ruthless People (Ruthless People, #1) by J.J. McAvoy" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1396504157s/21839603.jpg" alt="Ruthless People (Ruthless People, #1) by J.J.               <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=talk-dirty-to-me">talk-dirty-to-me</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer901879953" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer105469084663432279"><b>4 Exciting, Sizzling, Funny, Badass Stars!!!</b><br/><br/>Well colour me suprised!<br/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393592334ra/8736454.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>After seeing all my GR friends loving this book, I kind of got a bit of reverse performance anxiety. Because trust me, with my track record the chances of me enjoying a book everyone loved are very low. So I put reading this book off... but I finally stopped procrastinating and started reading it last night. Now I've always loved everything mob/mafia for as long as I've found the idea of a hot guy holding a gun hot. And I've al</span>
  <span id="freeText105469084663432279" style="display:none"><b>4 Exciting, Sizzling, Funny, Badass Stars!!!</b><br><br>Well colour me suprised!<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393592334ra/8736454.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After seeing all my GR friends loving this book, I kind of got a bit of reverse performance anxiety. Because trust me, with my track record the chances of me enjoying a book everyone loved are very low. So I put reading this book off... but I finally stopped procrastinating and started reading it last night. Now I've always loved everything mob/mafia for as long as I've found the idea of a hot guy holding a gun hot. And I've also read my fair share of mafia romances, and at some point the organised crime bit gets overshadowed by the romance and the characters. Imagine my surprise and elation when I realised that Ruthless People is about two crime families and their inner workings. Don't get me wrong, this book has all the right ingredients, it's gritty. Mcavoy tells us Liam and Melody's rather dark story but makes it palatable by using subtle humour. Making for an extremely satisfying read!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404405370i/10233995.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>He pulls a knife,<br>you pull a gun,<br>he sends one of yours to the hospital,<br>you send one of his to the morgue...<br>~Al Capone</i>
</b><br><br>This doesn't happen often but I freaking loved Melody's character! She's strong, bloody abrasive and doesn't take shit from anyone, normally I run at the first sign of her mouthing off, but dammit reading about her and Liam butting heads was amazing!<br><br>This book is filled with multifaceted characters. It's told in the first person with POV's from Liam and Melody but some of the other characters did get the odd POV, which gave the book more depth in my opinion.<br><br><i>
  <b>Rule One: You kill for family. You die for family. Because you can't trust anyone else.</b>
</i><br><br>Liam is next in line to take over the family business, all he has to do is marry the woman his father chose for him. No great feat, since Liam, would do just about anything to ensure the his place as the Ceann na Conairte. He doesn't care if his intended is ugly, the promise of power and respect are enough. They've never met, and Liam has no idea of what he should expect from Melody.<br><br><i>
  <b>Rule Four: No bloody divorce.</b>
</i><br><br>Let's just say, their first meeting is definitely one they will never forget! As much of a badass as Liam is, I think Melody dominated this story as the stronger character. Because ultimately Liam would do anything for her, and compromise he did! But... unlike other stories I've read where the hero becomes a pussy whipped weakling this did not happen in Liam's case, and thank God for that!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404406481i/10234258._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story is fast paced, and reads quite easily. And then's there's swearing, it's an art form people! I've read books where it's been done so badly I've cringed, but Liam and Melody swore so well, lol! <br><br>This was a very enjoyable debut from the author and I can't wait for more!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404407535i/10234368._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>ARC kindly provided by publisher on behalf of author via netgalley</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="105469084663432279" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_947226255" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/947226255" />
    <a title="Vanessa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12059859-vanessa"><img alt="Vanessa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576765878p2/12059859.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/947226255?book_show_action=true">May 24, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vanessa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vanessa" href="/user/show/12059859-vanessa">Vanessa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781612133201" href="/book/show/22237407-ruthless-people">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=not-just-no-but-fuck-no">not-just-no-but-fuck-no</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=rolling-my-eyes-out-of-my-head">rolling-my-eyes-out-of-my-head</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=drama-llama">drama-llama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=annoying-as-shit-heroines">annoying-as-shit-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=dnf">dnf</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer947226255" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2130276175803607808"><b>DNF @55% - 1 ARE YOU FUCKING KIDDING ME STAR!</b><br/><br/>Ughh... As much as this kills me because I was really looking forward to reading this series this weekend...just NO! <br/><br/>It's not every day that I have to pull this one out, but sometimes, it's just appropriate! <br/><br/><a href='http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/tumblr_lmouwix9Gx1qafrh6_zpsifhl0ihy.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421807890ra/13418651.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_lmouwix9Gx1qafrh6_zpsifhl0ihy.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>I will say, as I have said before on here, the mafia genre, especially Italian mafia, is one of my very favorites, in both film and books. So I am really picky when it comes to it, and I am expecting a lot when I read a book where the blurb cl</i></span>
  <span id="freeText2130276175803607808" style="display:none"><b>DNF @55% - 1 ARE YOU FUCKING KIDDING ME STAR!</b><br><br>Ughh... As much as this kills me because I was really looking forward to reading this series this weekend...just NO! <br><br>It's not every day that I have to pull this one out, but sometimes, it's just appropriate! <br><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/tumblr_lmouwix9Gx1qafrh6_zpsifhl0ihy.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421807890ra/13418651.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lmouwix9Gx1qafrh6_zpsifhl0ihy.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>I will say, as I have said before on here, the mafia genre, especially Italian mafia, is one of my very favorites, in both film and books. So I am really picky when it comes to it, and I am expecting a lot when I read a book where the blurb claims that it is like The Sopranos...one of my ALL TIME FAVORITE mafia shows! Right away you've set yourself up to meet some very high expectations!</i><br><br>In short, I found this book to be completely insulting to Irish and Italians everywhere. Do your research if you're going to try to write about modern day Italian and Irish mob life. Mel and Liam act like immature, uneducated assholes. They make mobsters look like they belong on Jerry Springer. They are basically running around and screaming, insulting each other, and/or shooting each other the whole time. <br><br>The story is completely OTT. This was BY FAR my largest problem with it. This combined with crappy show-vs-tell lacking writing, bad grammar, unbelievable dialogue, and don't even get me started on the <s>enemies to lovers</s> insta-love! Many of the plot lines were poorly developed as well. For example, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the attraction that DECLAN supposedly had for Mel <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> that was so overwhelming that it caused Coraline to confront Mel about it. She must've known about it too because she was quick to respond about it like it was common knowledge. Where the fuck did this come from? These characters had had multiple scenes together by this point where, this was in no way alluded to. Just very ametuer for me. :(<br><br>I <b> HATED</b> Mel with a vengeance. There is "ruthless" and then there is an unhinged fucking psychopath. I'll let you take a gander as to which one I found Mel to be. There was nothing good or redeeming about her. If I could murder her myself, I would. Infact...Mel? <br><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/Youre-Crazy-Reaction-Gif_zpszxtu6zi6.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427844086ra/14327456.gif" alt=" photo Youre-Crazy-Reaction-Gif_zpszxtu6zi6.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As for Liam, well I liked him in the beginning. He seemed sexy, enigmatic, and intriguing. But unfortunately, soon he started acting like an immature, spoiled little pussy-whipped bitch <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(what alpha male is fighting back the urge to tell his bitch of a wife that he loves her after just nine days of even knowing her??). Also, what alpha male asks his brother to shoot him in order to get some attention out of said bitch wife so that she will maybe admit that she loves him too? (&lt;----- Yeah, that was the scene that ended it all for me.) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I was half expecting for Mel to actually be the one with the dick when these two dropped trou but, I digress...<br><br>And speaking of dick, one word about the supposed hot and steamy sex scenes here....<b>RECYCLED!!</b><br>This is like a BAD wannabe rendition of 50 Shades and the Crossfire series, wrapped up under a mafia pretense. Nope, sorry...I actually wanted to read a REAL mafia book! <br><br>The majority of the Italian translations included throughout the book were incorrect. (Authors - STOP USING GOOGLE TRANSLATE!!!! It's inaccurate!) If you don't respect the language that you are trying to include in your book enough to make an effort for authenticity then I have no desire to support your work! Ughh! This is a pet peeve of mine. <br><br>A few specific examples of the OTT stuff that bothered me: <b>*WARNING* Spoilers from here to the end of the review</b><br><br>1) I already had to suspend some reality in order to believe that Mel (a woman) would be regarded as a mob boss. But, she had pretty much been doing it behind the scenes in place of her ailing father so, that I can believe, and I liked. However, to believe that an Irish and Italian mob boss would arrange a marriage of this sort for power unification is a BIG suspend belief request. These two cultures have loathed each other for decades. Again, I knew this going in so I am not faulting the book for this because it is part of the premise, and completely revealed in the blurb. But for her father to later admit that the driving force was actually so that she wouldn't be alone in life because he knows how lonely the life of a mob boss is? Yeah, I'm sorry no. Totally unrealistic.<br><br>2) The scene where Mel shoots and kills a pregnant woman for the sake of trying to get information out of someone. Ok, I am not in the mob myself so I am not going to claim to be some expert BUT, based on every single film, book, and documentary that I have ever seen, they preserve women, children, and the innocent at all costs. For a woman herself to do this? This didn't make me think that Mel was a bad ass. This made me despise her and made me want to shoot her in the face myself for being such a horrible, despicable, piece of shit individual. I am all for blood, gore, and darkness. This was not that. This was OTT shock factor bullshit. <br><br>3) The way that Liam speaks to the police Superintendent was completely OTT and unrealistic. In fact, that whole visit seemed unbelievable and cheesy to me. Basically he came over to say, hi, I'm the new guy and I am watching you, and you are going down, bitch! To which Liam's response was to once again scream, yell, threaten and throw a tantrum like a three-year-old. <br><br>4) The scene where Liam orders the take down of a commercial jet filled with smuggled drugs, once again, loaded with innocent women and children. Oh hey, btw...since when does the mafia and drug cartels smuggle cocaine and heroin via commercial jet liners?? I guess this amount of drugs just popped on right through security too, right? Because, absolutely nothing was explained there except for that the Valero had half a million dollars worth of coke and heroin stashed under their seats. <br><br>5) And the biggest bunch of bullshit of all - The scene where Mel shoots through a wall at a party filled with people to get to the men that were having a meeting without her, where she then SHOOTS a fucking mob boss???!!!???!!!????? I had to read this a few times to make sure that I didn't hallucinate it. ANYONE that ever takes a shot at a mob boss would be taken down, DEAD, in half a second, no questions asked. Sorry, that's where I completely checked out on hoping for any type of events that even remotely resembled realistic mob life. And yes, I know this is fiction and like I said before, I was willing to suspend a certain amount of reality to "go there" with the author but, The Sopranos was fiction. The Godfather was fiction. If you are going to put out a public work on a way of life, on a culture, I believe that you have a certain moral obligation towards research and on creating somewhat of an accurate portrayal. This was not that. This was like mafia gone white trash, trailer park, CRAZY!!!<br><br>I did love the concept behind this story and it is a shame that it wasn't executed properly. Again, I had super high hopes and am really upset as I know I am in the minority and many loved this series. I never ever DNF a book. I think this will be my third one, like ever. That's how much this one irked me. I feel used, insulted, and ripped off. Maybe it gets better but at his point, I am too pissed of and insulted to continue.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="2130276175803607808" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer962339839" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12073887926831068243"><b>4.5 **Motherfucking** Stars</b>..lol. Sorry for the language.. thats my inner Mel talking!!!<br/><b>"Mr. & Mrs. Smith meets the Sopranos..."</b><br/>Now..when I read that statement...my honest reaction was...<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403832461ra/10151253.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I mean come on...Sopranos...Mr & Mrs Smith..that's a tall order right there!!..But Im here to tell you...after reading this...I dont have a single suspicion...Ms .McAvoy absolutely...<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390753213ra/8273864.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Trust me people..<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403832461i/10151254._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403803169i/10146631.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Ruthless People</b> tells the story of <b>Liam Callahan</b> and <b>Melody Giovanni</b>..two powerful and ambitious individuals..tha</span>
  <span id="freeText12073887926831068243" style="display:none"><b>4.5 **Motherfucking** Stars</b>..lol. Sorry for the language.. thats my inner Mel talking!!!<br><b>"Mr. &amp; Mrs. Smith meets the Sopranos..."</b><br>Now..when I read that statement...my honest reaction was...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403832461ra/10151253.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I mean come on...Sopranos...Mr &amp; Mrs Smith..that's a tall order right there!!..But Im here to tell you...after reading this...I dont have a single suspicion...Ms .McAvoy absolutely...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390753213ra/8273864.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Trust me people..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403832461i/10151254._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403803169i/10146631.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Ruthless People</b> tells the story of <b>Liam Callahan</b> and <b>Melody Giovanni</b>..two powerful and ambitious individuals..that were brought together through an arranged marriage set up by their fathers when they were young..as a means to bring the two most fearless mafia families together..Without a question Liam and Melody are two of the most Ruthless People you will ever come across...It's not all sunny skies and rainbows with these two..their union resembles a tornado that tears up everything thing in its path....and I definitely had a...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403843544ra/10152524.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I loved the banter between them...they're both so head strong..it's comical how much these two are obviously meant for each other!!<br><a href="http://s1309.photobucket.com/user/Tempest989/media/imagejpg1_zpsd5343e6b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403832461i/10151256._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg1_zpsd5343e6b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403803169i/10146631.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Liam Callahan</b>-Boss of the Irish Mob..known as "The Boogeyman of the East"..but I like to refer to him as..**MR. MOD**<br><a href="http://s1309.photobucket.com/user/Tempest989/media/imagejpg1_zps29e80eea.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403844850i/10152639.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg1_zps29e80eea.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>He's cocky..feared..controlling..hot-tempered..and one sexy ass Alpha Male!!..There were scenes in this book where I wanted to throttle him..but the moment he went all Alpha with that dirty mouth..it was game over for me..yeap I was putty in his hands...<br><a href="http://s1309.photobucket.com/user/Tempest989/media/June/wik_adamlevine_zpsjbbd25kf.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403832461ra/10151258.gif" alt=" photo wik_adamlevine_zpsjbbd25kf.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403803169i/10146631.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Melody Giovanni</b>- Boss of the Italian mob..known as "The Wicked Witch of the West/Bloody Melody"...Yeap this chick got those names honestly and I loved her!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389116749ra/7991245.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Shes crazy..lol..theres no other way to describe her...she's one of those shoot now and dont ask questions later...definitely a Alpha female..cold..beautiful..an all around badass bitch..who has no problem putting any man in his place...<br><a href="http://s1309.photobucket.com/user/Tempest989/media/imagejpg1_zps10d812c1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403844850i/10152640.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg1_zps10d812c1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was <b>Ruthless People</b> in one gritty...down and dirty story..that I would happily recommend to my friends...so by all means pick this one up..you wont regret it!!<br><br>Ms.McAvoy...Bravo!!!..Strut your stuff woman..this one is pure gold!!<br><a href="http://s1309.photobucket.com/user/Tempest989/media/June/zQGMU_zpsm5ouic7w.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403832461ra/10151259.gif" alt=" photo zQGMU_zpsm5ouic7w.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>***ARC courtesy of publisher via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review***</b></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer924764450" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4027274949300678130"><b>5+ I Wanna be Mrs. Liam Callahan Stars!!</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406315557i/10534758._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><p><b>J.J. McAvoy</b> has created <b>Mr & Mrs Smith meets Goodfellas</b> in this brilliantly done novel. Ruthless People is one of my favorite reads of 2014!!! I'm a tiny bit ashamed of myself in saying this but, I totally rooted for the MC's and their ruthless, crazy, insane murderous ways!!</p><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406315557ra/10534759.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><p><b>What's this book about:</b><br/><b>Liam Alec Callahan</b>, is about to be the <i>Ceann na Conairte</i>, head of the Callahan Irish Mafia. Liam has it going on ladies: smart, charismatic, handsome, dominating</p></span>
  <span id="freeText4027274949300678130" style="display:none"><b>5+ I Wanna be Mrs. Liam Callahan Stars!!</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406315557i/10534758._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><p><b>J.J. McAvoy</b> has created <b>Mr &amp; Mrs Smith meets Goodfellas</b> in this brilliantly done novel. Ruthless People is one of my favorite reads of 2014!!! I'm a tiny bit ashamed of myself in saying this but, I totally rooted for the MC's and their ruthless, crazy, insane murderous ways!!</p><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406315557ra/10534759.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><p><b>What's this book about:</b><br><b>Liam Alec Callahan</b>, is about to be the <i>Ceann na Conairte</i>, head of the Callahan Irish Mafia. Liam has it going on ladies: smart, charismatic, handsome, dominating, and a voice that will melt your panties off. Of course, he's a man that will kill anyone who dares to get in his way or hurt his family! There's only a tiny stipulation, which he's known about since he was fifteen, Liam is arranged to be married to the daughter of the Italian mafia, Melody Nicci Giovanni. Liam is about to meet his match in every way.</p><br><p><b>Melody Nicci Giovanni</b>, daughter of the head of the Italian mafia, has a wee bit of a secret. She's not a meek, quiet, stepford wife and will <b>NOT</b> let some man tell her what she can or can not do. Melody has been the <i>Boss</i> for quite some time now while her father, Orlando Giovanni, fights to stay alive long enough to see his daughter get married and his mafia family merge with the Irish Callahan mafia. What could go wrong, right?</p><br><p><b>Buckle your seatbelts because you're in store for quite a ride!!</b> From the moment Liam &amp; Mel meet, things are not boring!! Liam attempts to put his wife-to-be in her place but of course Melody will have none of that.<br></p><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>He brushed his thumbs over my lips. "The moment the ink touched that fucking paper, you were mine. Mine to fuck. Mine to fucking command, and mine to put in your fucking place."<br><br>"First", I said, pressing into his neck, "get used to this position, because you're my bitch, not the other way around."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I loved the easy banter between these two. When they weren't fighting, their fucking was sizzling hot. Fighting for Liam &amp; Mel was some new form of foreplay. The fights these two would have had me envisioning Mr &amp; Mrs Smith while LMFAO at the same time.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406320942ra/10535479.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><p>They say the first year of marriage is the hardest. For Liam &amp; Mel, it is filled with challenges from a competing mafia family, a new police commissioner who is hell bent on cleaning up his city, betrayals, and of course, murder. The action in this book is fast paced and you will not want to join real life until you've read the very last page.</p><br><p>Yes....there is a bit of a surprise at the end but I didn't think it was earth shattering. I'm anxiously awaiting the next book in the series!!</p><br><p>
  <b>Thanks C.D. Canaries for another crazy fun Buddy Read!! MWAH!!</b>
</p><br><br><span>[image error]</span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11707727829934522394"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438716644i/15746567._SX540_.png' width='300' height='50' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>5 LIVIN*LOVEN*BLOODY*SEXY STARS!</b><br/><br/><b>"The Giovannis are one of the most powerful, if not the most powerful family in Italy and most of the west coast. My father wants an end to the rivalry between the Irish and the Italians."-Liam</b><br/><br/>Two households brought together to tear down the world! This is one mafia romance you will never forget! <br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431568131i/14849495.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Liam Callahan is the reigning prince of the Irish Mafia. In order to strengthen their power, Liam's father has arranged a marriage with Melody Giovanni the reigning Ita</span>
  <span id="freeText11707727829934522394" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438716644i/15746567._SX540_.png" width="300" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>5 LIVIN*LOVEN*BLOODY*SEXY STARS!</b><br><br><b>"The Giovannis are one of the most powerful, if not the most powerful family in Italy and most of the west coast. My father wants an end to the rivalry between the Irish and the Italians."-Liam</b><br><br>Two households brought together to tear down the world! This is one mafia romance you will never forget! <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431568131i/14849495.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Liam Callahan is the reigning prince of the Irish Mafia. In order to strengthen their power, Liam's father has arranged a marriage with Melody Giovanni the reigning Italian Mafia Princess. It should be so easy. He will take on a sweet wife to attend tea parties and keep his bed warm.<br><br><b>"With her family’s power added to my own, I would own it all before I was thirty."-Liam</b><br><br>Alas, Melody is NOT a princess. Melody is the queen. She has been running the family business for many years. She has no intention of baking and birthing babies. Melody wants to take over the world. She has no concern for others. She has no friends. She only has her kingdom and she RULES! She doesn't answer to anyone. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431573158i/14849894.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“Boogeyman of the East,” and I was the unknown “Wicked Witch of the West.”</b><br><br>Mel and Liam's first meeting is quite explosive. They begin a brutal push and pull. There is a battle of advance/retreat. The volatile spirits of these main characters can only be compared to a Sams club box of matches and a super sized gallon of gasoline! Although they both hold the keys to the kingdom, who will reign?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431573158i/14849895.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Do not kill. Do not kill. Melody, stay calm and do not kill him."<br> "But I would not let him win. I would not bow down to him. Not today. Not tomorrow. Not ever."<br>-Melody </b><br><br><b>"With that one shot, she had proven that breaking her was not possible. She would never convert to what I needed her to be. She was a ruthless savage, and if you cannot break a ruthless savage, you need to figure out how to tame them."-Liam</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431575200ra/14850135.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Liam comes up with a plan...<br><br> <b>"Step one, accept she was a damn boss. Step two, hide all the knives, guns, and maybe the pillows, too."-Liam </b><br><br>He is able to woo her with his charm. After all, he is a sexy Irish God! He holds the ability to show her love. He just has to win her over first.<br><br><b>“You are mine, as I am yours. But for this to work, you need to stop seeing me as a goddamned enemy and more like your husband.”-Liam</b><br><br>Liam and Mel come up with their own vows. With one goal in mind (dominate the human race) and the only probability to consider is to win or die trying. Kill or be killed. <br><br><b>“May we forever be rulers, may our enemies tremble at our feet, may we never forget our great love that is the family. Which we will rule with an iron fist. May we be ruthless and have no regrets. May we take what we want, when we want it, with the world at our feet.”-Mel</b><br><br>In addition to their truce, they find that they enjoy each other's bodies VERY MUCH! These two have passion. When they kill, when they go to bed, when they go to church, when they go for dinner, they do it with passion! They are both killers and lovers.<br><br><b>"No matter how many times I had her, it only made me want her even more."-Liam</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431574412i/14850050._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mel and Liam are violent and will stop at nothing to take down their enemies. Once these two have come together, hell hath no fury. They are focused on world domination and yet find time for tenderness with each other. <br><br><b>"God created her and then shattered the mold afterward, for the world could not handle two of her.”-Liam</b><br><br>Ruthless People is not a book for the weak hearted. It is over the top and the furnace is set on high burn for the entire read. Told in multiple POV, you dive deep into the souls of these characters. The witty banter and colorful text make this read beyond enjoyable. Once I started, I could not put it down. I love a read that evokes "the rainbow" of emotions! Mel was such a strong heroine. Even with her psychopath tendencies, I admired her. Was she crazy? Absolutely! I couldn't wait to see what she was going to do next. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431575360ra/14850193.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Liam Callahan is her perfect match. He is just as motivated to take on the world. But with Mel, his primary motivation becomes teaching her to love. He is the ultimate protector. He is able to heal her. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431574412i/14850051.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The secondary characters made this story complete. The diversity in each family member weaved tenderness, tension, happiness, joy, and peace within the chaos. How can I not fall in love with these people? <br><br>There is a moment in this book where my heart broke. I had to put it down to catch my breath. I was amazed at how quickly J.J. McAvoy was able to reengage my drive to continue the story. The heartbreak was painful but the healing was beautiful. The fury that followed still has my mind spinning.<br><br>I cannot rave enough about this book. I know many readers that did not enjoy living in this world. As for me, my bags are packed and I'm ready to move in. I will be on to the second book very soon. <br><br><b>BR IN HONOR OF OUR STRONG MAFIA QUEEN Sasha Elle with the ladies of Shh… [Smut, Heroes &amp; HEAs…].....Thanks for inviting me to the party!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431573158i/14849896._SY540_.jpg" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:</b><br><a href="http://craziesrusbookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434387282i/15214674._SX540_.jpg" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="11707727829934522394" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_907180698" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/907180698" />
    <a title="Amanda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7451210-amanda"><img alt="Amanda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1434101513p2/7451210.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/907180698?book_show_action=true">Apr 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amanda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amanda" href="/user/show/7451210-amanda">Amanda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7451210-amanda?shelf=kickass-badass-hero">kickass-badass-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7451210-amanda?shelf=funny-hilarious">funny-hilarious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7451210-amanda?shelf=favourite-2014">favourite-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7451210-amanda?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7451210-amanda?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7451210-amanda?shelf=funny-hero">funny-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7451210-amanda?shelf=arc-netgalley">arc-netgalley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer907180698" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6850651455500663665"><b>Everyone is ruthless. They just don't know it. You do. I do. And that is why we are on top and will remain so."</b><br/><br/>Oh, to hell with it, I will just go with the 5 stars. Freedom of rating and all that. I don't care that the main character should have rot in hell for the things they did, I grew to root for the Callahan's clan. I can't believe this is actually a debut novel, it was faced-paced, action packed, entertaining, sexy and exhilarating. <br/><br/>We have two main characters that very much resembles Mr. </span>
  <span id="freeText6850651455500663665" style="display:none"><b>Everyone is ruthless. They just don't know it. You do. I do. And that is why we are on top and will remain so."</b><br /><br />Oh, to hell with it, I will just go with the 5 stars. Freedom of rating and all that. I don't care that the main character should have rot in hell for the things they did, I grew to root for the Callahan's clan. I can't believe this is actually a debut novel, it was faced-paced, action packed, entertaining, sexy and exhilarating. <br /><br />We have two main characters that very much resembles Mr. and Mrs. Smith. Yes, I kid you not, just minus the mundane house chore and add more blood and gore into it. Melody was seriously a scary bitch and Liam was immature and hotheaded. He might just blew you up for the heck of it. I also love that the author emphasize a lot on the mafia business front and the mayhem they plot together. This husband and wife was a force to be reckoned with. Don't messed with them. <br /><br />The title really suits and painted the right picture for the couple, they are the Ruthless People. Yes, no one has any heart of gold, just so you know. So don't expect romantic notion, swoony moments, flowery stuff or any honorable characters.<br /><br />At first, I really disliked both Liam and Mel. They were each a bastard and a bitch. You might be thinking what a match made in heaven. Well, if they didn't rip off each other throat first. The way Liam treated his booty call was super douche at best. He was like a child in a man's body, cocky, immature, hotheaded and impatient to step up to be the boss man. Even though he had no idea how his future wife looks like, as long as he is going to be the next in line for the title, he is going to marry an ogre if that's what it takes.<br /><br />Melody Giovanni is also scary bitch. She's the kind of woman who make grown man weep. She is not looking forward to be Liam's arm candy or a dutiful wife either.<br /><br /><b>"I would rather shoot you, but since I can't, I will sexually frustrate you instead. Do not rip my clothing."<br />"Bitch is going to kill me."</b><br /><br />Honestly, if both of them got ambushed and murdered by the Valero, I don't think I would have shed a tear.<br /><br />Initially, I was hoping that their hatred for each other to last a little longer considering this is going to be a trilogy. When they reached an unanimous agreement to work out their marriage and RULE the world together, I thought it was a nice change because there was only so much fight I can't take between these two alpha beings. Each wanted to top the other and they finally agree to a pact. Everything works out great by the way.<br /><br /><b>"What do you say, my Mel? We end our war and join brains and bodies and destroy any against us. We become one ruthless person instead of two."</b><br /><br />Either I was feeling acclimatize to their way of life or they were getting more likable because they were seriously growing on me, I was kinda rooting for them to be the mafia king and queen and killed off the Valero.<br /><br />I didn't read a lot of mafia story, but this one really did encompassed a lot of mafia business, the drama, the family, the cruelty and ruthlessness in it. They were a bunch of unapologetic scum and I don't even to look for their redeeming qualities.<br /><br />Their relationship did resemble Mr. and Mrs. Smith. Both wanted to be the alpha, but we know who is the brain and who is the brawn in this relationship. This dynamic duo was fantastic, Mel was all straight to the point, efficient and discipline, Liam was all impromptu, manipulative and cunning. There were times that Liam felt emasculated by his wife. Poor him. But he did have his time to shine at the rare opportunity. Liam provided too much laugh out loud moment for me even though he was torturing and killing off people. Some of it is a tad comical, but it was freaking hilarious. <br /><br />Although this is the first of a trilogy, I don't feel like I have an incomplete story. In the end, it was a very satisfying story that left me begging for more next. Definitely worth to read it without waiting for the next one.<br /><br />P/s: In order to enjoy this one, you definitely should be able to handle reading about your H/h killing enemies and innocent alike without any remorse whatsoever. <br /><br /><b>"This was how it should have been from the start. She and I setting the world on fire together."</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="6850651455500663665" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

Even the real mafia. <br><br><br>I thought Liam was sexy in the beginning but as soon as he started acting pussy whipped, I was turned off. He acted like the woman in that<br>relationship. It was hard to take him seriously as the <b>"Ceann na Conairte"</b>, which is the Irish Mafia's equivalent to the <b>Godfather</b> of the Italian Mafia.<br><br><br>I'll give the author points for originality, since I have never read a story like this before. I just didn't enjoy reading this one. I battled with wanting to DNF the book, but after wasting three days on it, I was determined to finish it.<br><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_1950872937" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1950872937" />
    <a title="MischaS_" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12772859-mischas"><img alt="MischaS_" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585808485p2/12772859.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1950872937?book_show_action=true">Mar 27, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MischaS_" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MischaS_" href="/user/show/12772859-mischas">MischaS_</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12772859-mischas?shelf=best-girls-ever">best-girls-ever</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12772859-mischas?shelf=butchering-a-foreign-language">butchering-a-foreign-language</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12772859-mischas?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12772859-mischas?shelf=best-book-in-the-series">best-book-in-the-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12772859-mischas?shelf=best-books-ever">best-books-ever</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12772859-mischas?shelf=best-men-ever">best-men-ever</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1950872937" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11448762075621928694">EDIT (17/12/2018): I officially need to stop learning new languages! A couple of months ago I started with Italian, and it managed to destroy a book for me, already! Okay, the thing is, Melody is Italian, and several times she or another character speak Italian. The author several times said that she had it multiple times checked to make sure those sentences are correct. But I can say that she did not! I can see those mistakes. <br/>And I love this book or even the whole series. But honestly, I'm jus</span>
  <span id="freeText11448762075621928694" style="display:none">EDIT (17/12/2018): I officially need to stop learning new languages! A couple of months ago I started with Italian, and it managed to destroy a book for me, already! Okay, the thing is, Melody is Italian, and several times she or another character speak Italian. The author several times said that she had it multiple times checked to make sure those sentences are correct. But I can say that she did not! I can see those mistakes. <br />And I love this book or even the whole series. But honestly, I'm just angry with another series because the author butchered Russian there. And it is not fair to give this book a free pass just because I like it. I can recognise that the other author managed to butcher the language in a couple of words. McAvoy is failing on longer sentences. However, I'm telling you, it is better to have no Italian (or any language you do not know) than butcher the language. <br />Also, because I read this book several times, I know it, and with every re-read, I see more and more typos, nonsense sentences and switches in the scenes. Like Mel wearing a dress, suddenly it's a t-shirt, and on the next page, it's a dress once again. <br />I love McAvoy and her books because the characters are just so ruthless. However, she needs a better editor! And a native Italian. <br /><br />In regards to me a little revelation, I need to lower the rating. But I can honestly say that if it was my first read, I saw the bad Italian I would be angrier. However, since I already have a little connection to the story, I'm going to be a bit nicer. (4/5 ⭐)<br /><br /><br />EDIT: I had to change the rating because this one is my favourite in the series. (5/5 ⭐)<br /><br />ORIGINAL: This just randomly appeared in my Goodreads Updates Feed, and I knew I had to read it. So, I put it in my To Read shelf and move one. But some little devil was sitting on my shoulder and screaming to read it right away. And I did. (4/5 ⭐)<br /><br /><b>Love this because they are really bad guys and openly evil. And they own it. There is no good vs evil. This is about who's the biggest evil of them all!</b><br />Finally! I waited so long for a book where the characters would just own that they are not good or pretend there is some higher good they do evil things for. <br /><br />I don't say this very often. But I loved the main heroine. Melody was everything. Rude. Smart. Wicked. Evil. Cold. And much more. But mainly - She was a boss from start to finish. I love how at their first meeting she came on top. Knowing more then the Callahans did. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ And honestly? I loved that she was so violent. Like actually firing at him!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Liam was an idiot. But amazing idiot! I loved that his little "man-only" word was turned around. <br /><br />What I really liked about this was the dynamics. Usually in books like this book you got an evil man and weeping flower. Or if she is some sort of leader, she, thanks to her love for the man, realises that she doesn't want to be like that and hands him all the power. No, they were a match set in hell. <br /><br />Also, Fedel is sooo damn cute! I want to see more of him.<br /><br />And I have to have some negatives. <br />- <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Really, getting pregnant? That fast? I thought she was using a pill or something? But okay when she got pregnant, I knew something would happen to the baby. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />- The Liam's little play to make sure <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ she loves him real and forever  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> was a bit theatrical. But okay.<br />- Was this a Twilight fan fiction? Because I got a bit of that vibe. Especially with the characters in the family.<br />Even the Melody/Olivia hate was sort of Bella/Rosalie...<br />But maybe I am seeing things that do not exist. :D<br />- Olivia needs a good death. And quickly. She's getting on my nerves.<br />- Some typos - not a grammar nazi. I know that I have a lot of typos and grammar mistakes, and usually I just do not realise it. But when even I see them in a book? That's not good.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11448762075621928694" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_904549476" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/904549476?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time">*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=arc">arc</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer904549476" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7575158860127812434">4.5--<b>Ruthless</b>--Stars!!!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"You kill for family. You die for family. Because you can't trust anyone else."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/>The <b>merging</b> of two powerhouse families.<br/><br/>The <b>uniting</b> of the Irish and the Italian. <br/><br/>The <b>marriage</b> of the Boss and the Ceann na Conairte.<br/><br/>The <b>joining</b> of the Wicked Witch of the West and the Boogeyman of the East. <br/><br/><b>Liam Alec Callahan</b> and <b>Melody Nicci Giovanni</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386694182ra/7421082.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Together Liam and Melody will rule the world. They will take down the Valero. They will elimate anyone that stands in their way. They w</span>
  <span id="freeText7575158860127812434" style="display:none">4.5--<b>Ruthless</b>--Stars!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"You kill for family. You die for family. Because you can't trust anyone else."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>The <b>merging</b> of two powerhouse families.<br><br>The <b>uniting</b> of the Irish and the Italian. <br><br>The <b>marriage</b> of the Boss and the Ceann na Conairte.<br><br>The <b>joining</b> of the Wicked Witch of the West and the Boogeyman of the East. <br><br><b>Liam Alec Callahan</b> and <b>Melody Nicci Giovanni</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386694182ra/7421082.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Together Liam and Melody will rule the world. They will take down the Valero. They will elimate anyone that stands in their way. They will kill. They will bleed. They will fight to protect their family. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"May we forever be rulers. May our enemies tremble at our feet, may we never forget our great love that is the family. Which we will rule with an iron fist."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>That is if Liam and Melody can survive each other. Liam thought he was getting a nice compliant wife. One that would bow to his wishes. That would stand by and support his decisions. A wife he could control. Instead he got Melody.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435689ra/880361.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Melody is used to ruling her empire. She doesn't take shit from anyone. Not even her new husband. She's never had a partner. Someone to share her role with, her life with. She's never loved anyone. <br><br>Marrying Liam changes everything for Melody.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I want you to love me. But if not, then I want it to be the closest thing to you loving me. I want your loyalty. I want your honesty. I want you by my side and no one else's. I want your body. I want your mind. I want to know your hopes and dreams so I could one day make them reality."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>This was gritty. It was violent. It was bloody. It was dangerous. It was the crime world at it's best. <br><br>I loved the banter between Liam and Melody. How they fought over who wore the pants in the relationship. Who was stronger. Who was more ruthless. Who would come out on top. How they realized that they were stronger together. More powerful. Beyond ruthless. Unstoppable.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387222702ra/7553867.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Talk about action packed as Liam and Melody fight to bring down the Valero. <br><br>Betrayal. <br>Revenge. <br>Vengeance. <br>Retaliation.<br><br>Liam and Melody will have to work together. To trust each other. Their newly formed marriage will be tested. Lives will be lost. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I was the king of the jungle, and the woman beside me was my queen."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>I was enthralled. I couldn't stop reading. I loved the characters. The banter was great. There was action. There was steam. <br><br><b>WARNING:</b> This is book one of a trilogy. Honestly, aside from the epilogue this one <i>could</i> be read as a standalone. The epilogue opened things up. I'm not raging for the next book, but I will definitely be stalking NetGalley for it. <br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided by The Writer's Coffee Shop Publishing House via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review</i>
</b></span>

</b><br><br>I mean for realz yo. When I read that I was seriously like . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459186092ra/18579907.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Or momma. Whatevs.<br><br>Meet Melody Giovanni and Liam Callahan. She’s the daughter of the Italian mob boss. He’s the son of the Irish version. The two have been made an offer they can’t refuse – an arranged marriage which will bring the two families together so they can <b>really</b> run Chicago. Liam expects a new missus who will spend her days shopping, attending charity events and the like. Melody expects her days to be spent doing things that are <i>juuuuuuuuust</i> a bit different from her hubbie’s plans . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>What neither ever imagined was . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I mean these two seriously knew how to go 'head girl go 'head get down and I was all: Praise Jeebus! Me pantaloons – they doth disintegrate. <br><br>If you like your porno with a real poopton of torture and your MCs to be bad to the bone, this is most definitely the selection for you. If you are <s>a flippin’ nutter</s> one of the abundance of 1-Star reviewers for <i>Ruthless People</i> who expect their pornography to be "a realistic depiction of the mafia," you should probably just fuck off because seriously? <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459186092ra/18579910.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Don’t harsh my buzz. Porn is not real. I don't have a super drippy honeypot and none of my friends admits to having one either. Also? If someone tried to stick it up my butt without even a warning? Hell to the nah - he'd be going to the emergency room to get his ding-dong sewn back on. Reality has <b>ZERO</b> place in these stories. Just ask my hubs 'cause when I read a "real" story I get all "BUT THAT WOULD NEVER HAPPEN AND OH MY GOD I'M GOING TO STRAP DYNAMITE TO THIS STUPID SONOFABITCH AND BLOW IT UP WHEN I'M DONE READING IT!" but when I read porn I'm all . . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>And he likey. (Mitchell? Notsamuch.)<br><br>(3.5 Stars if I could because if you're going to charge people $5.00 for something, there really shouldn't be so many typos and also because really with the instalove? You're damn lucky my underwears exploded from the smexy parts and made me fuggetaboutit.)<br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7629922433330805283"><b>WHEN I READ THIS BLURB:</b> <br/>Ruthless People is a<b> romantic crime fiction set in modern day Chicago,</b> and follows the life and marriage of Melody Giovanni and Liam Callahan—<b>rivals by blood and leaders through fear. </b><br/>I knew I wanted to read this book. Thank you, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha' rel='nofollow noopener'>SueBee</a>, for sharing Liam with me. *muah* ♥<br/><br/><b>
  <u>RULES:</u>
</b><br/><br/>✦<b>ONE</b> You kill for family. You die for family. Because you can't trust anyone else.<br/><br/>✦<b>TWO</b> Take no prisoners and have no regrets about it.<br/><br/>✦<b>THREE</b> Just because you sell drugs for a living isn't an exc</span>
  <span id="freeText7629922433330805283" style="display:none"><b>WHEN I READ THIS BLURB:</b> <br>Ruthless People is a<b> romantic crime fiction set in modern day Chicago,</b> and follows the life and marriage of Melody Giovanni and Liam Callahan—<b>rivals by blood and leaders through fear. </b><br>I knew I wanted to read this book. Thank you, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha" rel="nofollow noopener">SueBee</a>, for sharing Liam with me. *muah* ♥<br><br><b>
  <u>RULES:</u>
</b><br><br>✦<b>ONE</b> You kill for family. You die for family. Because you can't trust anyone else.<br><br>✦<b>TWO</b> Take no prisoners and have no regrets about it.<br><br>✦<b>THREE</b> Just because you sell drugs for a living isn't an excuse not to dress well.<br><br>✦<b>FOUR</b> No bloody divorce.<br><br>(...)<br><br>✦<b>SIXTEEN</b> Never displease your mother. <i>*I personally like this rule.* </i><br><br>A small portion of <b>Ruthless People</b> took place in <b>Cascadia, Oregon</b>. Location wise that is about an hour northeast of me. I was pleasantly surprised to see this beautiful forested area was mentioned. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406269061i/10528119._SY540_.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>"May we forever be rulers, may our enemies tremble at our feet, may we never forget our great love that is the family. Which we will rule with an iron fist. May we be ruthless and have no regrets. May we take what we want, when we want it, with the world at our feet."</blockquote><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21839603.Ruthless_People__Ruthless_People___1_" title="Ruthless People (Ruthless People, #1) by J.J. McAvoy" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22237428.The_Untouchables__Ruthless_People___2_" title="The Untouchables (Ruthless People, #2) by J.J. McAvoy" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1400640213s/22237428.jpg" alt="The Untouchables (Ruthless People, #2) by J.J. McAvoy" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22237681.American_Savages__Ruthless_People___3_" title="American Savages (Ruthless People, #3) by J.J. McAvoy" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts">Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781612133201" href="/book/show/22237407-ruthless-people">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer955831394" class="readable"
