<span id="freeTextContainer12658574604114782725">It's LIVE!<br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.amazon.co.uk/Ruthless-People-J-J-McAvoy-ebook/dp/B00LVA6QYM/ref=sr_1_2?s=books&ie=UTF8&qid=1405605272&sr=1-2&keywords=ruthless+people'>http://www.amazon.co.uk/Ruthless-Peop...</a><br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.amazon.com/Ruthless-People-J-J-McAvoy-ebook/dp/B00LVA6QYM/ref=sr_1_1?s=digital-text&ie=UTF8&qid=1405605164&sr=1-1&keywords=ruthless+people'>http://www.amazon.com/Ruthless-People...</a><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402050582i/9887622.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ruthless People has Power struggles, conflict, Mafia bosses, an arranged marriage, sex, romance, rivals, love.... It's a Ruthless Story about Ruthless people, and never has a title been more apt. <br/><br/><b>“Everyone is ruthless. They just don’t know it.”</b><br/><br/>Three families are stronger than all the rest; their names feared by many...<br/><b>Callaghan <br/>Giovannis <br/>Valero</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Who will reign supreme?</i>
</b><br/><br/>Two families join together in marriag</span>
  <span id="freeText12658574604114782725" style="display:none">It's LIVE!<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/Ruthless-People-J-J-McAvoy-ebook/dp/B00LVA6QYM/ref=sr_1_2?s=books&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1405605272&amp;sr=1-2&amp;keywords=ruthless+people">http://www.amazon.co.uk/Ruthless-Peop...</a><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Ruthless-People-J-J-McAvoy-ebook/dp/B00LVA6QYM/ref=sr_1_1?s=digital-text&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1405605164&amp;sr=1-1&amp;keywords=ruthless+people">http://www.amazon.com/Ruthless-People...</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402050582i/9887622.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ruthless People has Power struggles, conflict, Mafia bosses, an arranged marriage, sex, romance, rivals, love.... It's a Ruthless Story about Ruthless people, and never has a title been more apt. <br><br><b>“Everyone is ruthless. They just don’t know it.”</b><br><br>Three families are stronger than all the rest; their names feared by many...<br><b>Callaghan <br>Giovannis <br>Valero</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Who will reign supreme?</i>
</b><br><br>Two families join together in marriage to form an unbeatable alliance. A force greater than any before or after..... <i>A powerhouse mafia.</i> That's the intention but <b>what would be the reality?</b><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404246895i/10213813._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>They had to make it work. </i><br><br><u>The bride...</u><br><b>Melody Nicci Giovanni, 24</b><br>She lost her mother during childhood in tragic circumstances. Mel's father, Orlando, single-handedly raised her in a protective bubble and made her into the ruthless cold hearted, harsh, standoffish bitch that she needs to be.... <b>The Boss</b> <i>“…the most beautiful woman I had ever seen….. I could tell she was perfection.”</i> Mel is the definition of <i>badassery...</i> She's <i>ruthless</i> through and through. There's nothing she will not do to show her power....<i> Nothing </i> <br><br><u>...and groom.</u><br><b>Liam Alec Callaghan, 27 </b><br>He has an expectation of how he thinks his wife should behave....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404249845i/10214368.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He’s immature, impatient, aggressive, cocky, arrogant, chauvinistic and possessive. <i>How will his bride feel about all of this? </i>Will Liam be able to tame her to bend to his will and be the wife he imagines worthy of the most powerful Mafia leader? <b> “There was one boss, only one Ceann na Conairte, and it was not her.”</b><br><br>And herein lies a major conflict with the <b>Ruthless People</b>, who will reign supreme within the alliance..… Can they come to an agreement, in order to <i>dominate?</i> <br><br>They're aggressive, they fight, have power struggles, even when they're having explosive HOT sex. The author is completely consistent with their personalities and behaviour. There’s an undeniable intense attraction between them and that's what<b> I love most about this story, the relationship between Mel and Liam. </b> What a character team! I wanted to experience their every thought, and every word, whilst they were together, because together they're dynamite.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404223836i/10209752.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Can she trust him?</i><br><br>There are a ton of additional characters in the story, lots of family and links within the families, it was hard for me to keep track of at times, and maybe affected the story pacing for me, just a little, but, equally, I think this story requires the layers all the additional characters provide.<br><br><b>No one was safe from their goal to reign supreme.</b><br><br>They feel no remorse, no guilt about their murderous, violent activities. <b>They. Are. Ruthless.</b> Even in their innermost thoughts, especially Mel, she's a force to be reckoned with. <i>She does not allow her heart to feel. </i><br><br><b>Ruthless People</b> felt completely different to books I usually read and that was refreshing but I would've liked to see more of their vulnerable side, I caught glimpses but I needed a little more light and shade, and not just with each other. If I'm completely honest, I don’t think I truly connected to the characters until near the end of the story but I don’t wish to take away the brilliance of this dynasty. I've a feeling that the next book will probably fulfill this desire in me! <br><br>The story that evolves and the characters who unravel before us are gripping. I wasn't always sure that I liked the them, sometimes I did and sometimes I didn't....<i> But</i> I enjoyed the Mafia reading experience, so 4 stars from me! And the ending, well, I wasn't expecting <i>that</i> to happen! If you like the sound of what this story has to offer go grab your copy and enjoy the crazy mafia ride with Mel and Liam! <br><br><i>I can't wait for more!</i><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402051113ra/9887660.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>ARC kindly provided by The Writer's Coffee Shop Publishing House, via NetGalley, in exchange for an honest review<br></span>

<div id="review_905864839" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/905864839" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/905864839?book_show_action=true">Apr 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=5-stars-favorites">5-stars-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer905864839" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3271434510673506032"><b>ADD THIS TO YOUR TBR LIST... IT's HELLA GOOD</b><br/><br/><b>5 Kickin’ Booty Stars</b><br/> <br/><b>I love coming across a new author and I love it when I love the book! Ruthless People is very much like Mr. & Mrs. Smith with a touch of mafia</b><br/> <br/>There are a few things you should know…<br/> <br/>- The Hero and Heroine are Ruthless People.<br/>- The Hero is Irish<br/>- The Heroine is Italian <br/>- Both are to be wed and both are fine with it<br/>- Both want to be the boss and therefore, there’s lots of juicy and yummy drama!<br/> <br/><b>Summary</b><br/> <br/>Very early on, Liam and Melod</span>
  <span id="freeText3271434510673506032" style="display:none"><b>ADD THIS TO YOUR TBR LIST... IT's HELLA GOOD</b><br><br><b>5 Kickin’ Booty Stars</b><br> <br><b>I love coming across a new author and I love it when I love the book! Ruthless People is very much like Mr. &amp; Mrs. Smith with a touch of mafia</b><br> <br>There are a few things you should know…<br> <br>- The Hero and Heroine are Ruthless People.<br>- The Hero is Irish<br>- The Heroine is Italian <br>- Both are to be wed and both are fine with it<br>- Both want to be the boss and therefore, there’s lots of juicy and yummy drama!<br> <br><b>Summary</b><br> <br>Very early on, Liam and Melody are expected to wed. Liam is the son of the Irish mafia boss and Melody is the daughter of the Italian boss. Both fathers made this deal in order to join the two sides and create a bigger entity. The only problem, both Liam and Melody want to be “the” boss.<br> <br><b>Melody</b><br> <br>It’s difficult for me to like a strong Heroine because sometimes they can come off as kind of mean and not likeable. I, however, do like Melody. She reminds me a lot like Sarai in Killing Sarai. Melody was born into this mafia life and without anyone to rely on, but herself she does what she needs to do. She can fight, she isn’t scared of anyone and doesn’t blink an eye if she needs to kill…. even if it’s innocent people.<br> <br><b>Liam</b><br><br>Liam may be marrying a strong woman, but that doesn’t mean Liam is weak. Liam has to prove his worth and just like Melody he isn’t afraid to show people that he is the man and he will do anything it takes to protect his family and business. He will kill, torture and backstab anyone who gets in his way.<br> <br><b>Melody and Liam Dynamics</b><br> <br>The thing I love most about this couple is that they both were okay getting married. That wasn’t the “issue” of the book. I also love how strong both characters are. Melody at times did frustrate me because she was pretty suborn and was very determine to be set in her ways. Liam is the sexy Hero I love to read. He’s powerful, cocky and at the same time very endearing. Liam shows more affection in the book and it just makes your heart swoon.<br> <br><b>The ups and downs and all around</b><br><br>Ruthless People isn’t a difficult book to read, but it’s not a simple book. Not like most tame mafia books, Melody and Liam do go into business by selling drugs, weapons and at times innocent people are killed. I know, sometimes you wish mafia people are “nice” and only do nice business transaction, but I think the author was trying to make the characters as raw as possible and it didn’t bother me.<br> <br>Also, the language of the book can be a bit distracting for some people. I don’t really mind all the F and cuss words, but that is just me. I did feel like there was a bit too much threating to kill. Many times Melody would say she would rather kill so and so than do this and Liam would do the same. The first few times were okay, but it started to become sprinkled throughout the book and I just kind of wanted them to stop saying it and just focus on the task at hand.<br> <br>Overall, I really enjoyed Ruthless People. It had everything I looked for in a mafia type of book, there was plenty of action, sexual tension and ruthless killing. <br> <br>A MUST READ!<br><br><i>An ARC was provided in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21839603.Ruthless_People__Ruthless_People___1_" title="Ruthless People (Ruthless People, #1) by J.J. McAvoy" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1396504157s/21839603.jpg" alt="Ruthless People (Ruthless People, #1) by J.J. McAvoy" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00LVA6QYM/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;creativeASIN=B00LVA6QYM&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=jacqsread-20&amp;linkId=GJCX6X5DHDYEOJEM" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422563800i/13517114.gif" width="1" height="1" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

<div id="review_924385888" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/924385888" />
    <a title="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14351108-deanna-pink-lady"><img alt="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1370640721p2/14351108.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/924385888?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" href="/user/show/14351108-deanna-pink-lady">Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14351108-deanna-pink-lady?shelf=hot-and-sexy">hot-and-sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14351108-deanna-pink-lady?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14351108-deanna-pink-lady?shelf=bad-boys">bad-boys</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer924385888" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3612007769336734245"><b> 4.5 "Ruthless" Stars</b> <br/><br/>The Irish and the Italian....The Ceann na Conairte and The Boss....the "Boogeyman of the East" and the unknown "Wicked Witch of the West." Liam Alec Callahan from Chicago and Melody "Mel" Nicci Giovanni from California have been preordained to be married by their fathers. It would join the Irish and the Italian mafia, the biggest merger the mafia world would ever see. The only catch, which runs the show? This book is about the mafia, they kill, sell drugs, and manipulate at</span>
  <span id="freeText3612007769336734245" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 "Ruthless" Stars</b> <br><br>The Irish and the Italian....The Ceann na Conairte and The Boss....the "Boogeyman of the East" and the unknown "Wicked Witch of the West." Liam Alec Callahan from Chicago and Melody "Mel" Nicci Giovanni from California have been preordained to be married by their fathers. It would join the Irish and the Italian mafia, the biggest merger the mafia world would ever see. The only catch, which runs the show? This book is about the mafia, they kill, sell drugs, and manipulate at all cost to rule. (I for one LOVED the Sopranos so this book got me all tingly)<br><br><i>Family is everything.<br>Rule One: You kill for family. You die for family. Because you can't trust anyone else.<br>Rule Two: Take no prisoners and have no regrets about it.<br>Rule Three: Just because you sell drugs for a living isn't an excuse not to dress well.</i><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Quotes/Ruthlesspeople_zps73cb43bf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402891015i/10007967._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Ruthlesspeople_zps73cb43bf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Liam and Mel are both feisty, headstrong, fierce, brave, cut-throat leaders. They kill, steal, and do whatever it takes to get the job done. They never back down and what they do best is lead. In a perfect mafia marriage, the wife stays quiet, looks beautiful and stands behind her man. But what happens when your wife is <b>The Boss</b> of her group and is use to doing things her way and has NO desire to play second fiddle to her husband? Well you get fireworks, explosions, very heated "discussions", and an occasional gunshot. <br><br><b>"The strongest survive, however, and the key to survival is to evolve with your environment. We have evolved, the mafia has evolved, and now it's your turn. Melody Giovanni is your evolution, embrace it and make peace."</b><br><br>Mel is kick ass and I loved her from the beginning. She is harsh and brash but she has many walls built around her, it's her only way of survival. Liam in all his arrogance and cockiness sees how perfect they are for one another. He has to tear down her wall and it's not an easy thing to do. <br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Quotes/liam1_zps2f2cd0c8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402899395i/10009919._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo liam1_zps2f2cd0c8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The back and forth between Liam and Mel was spot on. Their love/hate feelings for one another were funny at times, touching at times and downright combustible at times. Their sexual chemistry was lustful, animalistic, and passionate.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402892241ra/10008073.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love how they grow as a couple. Both breaking down barriers and realizing that they are so similar in nature that they both truly understand each other down to their core. Learning to give and take-learning to love and trust one another. Plotting together and forging one family united. <br><br>When their world is turned upside down and tragedy strikes, how they deal with it and what was done to help them cope was sweet and endearing. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I loved how all the family members told Mel secrets trying to get her to talk. While Mel was ruthless, how she coped with her tragedy showed that deep down she was emotional and loving. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> The family rallies around them because that's what family does.<br> <a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Quotes/Liam_zps6dd89a3f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402895250i/10008932._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo Liam_zps6dd89a3f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I loved all the secondary characters. They added lots of flavor to the story. I liked the twist and turns the story took us on and the end just had me licking my chops for the next book. The story does not have a cliffy but you are anxious for the wild ride that Liam and Mel have ahead of them. I for one can't wait for the next book!!<br><br>JJ-<br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Gifs/AngieHarmonThankYou_zps493c750c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386046010ra/7279620.gif" alt=" photo AngieHarmonThankYou_zps493c750c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>for so graciously gifting me an ARC for an honest review. I honestly loved your book!!<br><br>BR with Jxxx, TeriLyn, Mo and Irene and with the occasional stalking from SueBee and Bev. ♥♥<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="3612007769336734245" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_905445008" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/905445008" />
    <a title="MELISSA *Mel Reader*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10312276-melissa-mel-reader"><img alt="MELISSA *Mel Reader*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1517366723p2/10312276.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/905445008?book_show_action=true">Apr 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MELISSA *Mel Reader*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MELISSA *Mel Reader*" href="/user/show/10312276-melissa-mel-reader">MELISSA *Mel Reader*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10312276-melissa-mel-reader?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer905445008" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16315299562097484365">4.5 "Stupid Fucking Sexy Irish Man" Stars!<br/>(ARC provided by Netgalley)<br/><br/><a href='http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/1ecce01a-4cd6-44d8-8316-fd3b7b119c58.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404614098i/10264368.jpg' alt=' photo 1ecce01a-4cd6-44d8-8316-fd3b7b119c58.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/d17d0161-dba0-4a06-8a82-857979689c76.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404605630i/10263483.jpg' alt=' photo d17d0161-dba0-4a06-8a82-857979689c76.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Melody Nicci Giovanni aka Mel/Boss/Bloody Melody is a 24 yr. old badass woman who was raised to rule the Italian Mafia, and be the 1st female boss. The Giovanni's are one of the most powerful families in Italy, and on the west coast.<br/><br/><a href='http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/agungif.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404608769ra/10263777.gif' alt=' photo agungif.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Melody is the only child to mob boss Orlando Giovanni, and he trained her since the age of 7 to be fearless, ruthless, & powerful. To show no mercy, and lead through fear. As a woman in </span>
  <span id="freeText16315299562097484365" style="display:none">4.5 "Stupid Fucking Sexy Irish Man" Stars!<br>(ARC provided by Netgalley)<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/1ecce01a-4cd6-44d8-8316-fd3b7b119c58.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404614098i/10264368.jpg" alt=" photo 1ecce01a-4cd6-44d8-8316-fd3b7b119c58.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/d17d0161-dba0-4a06-8a82-857979689c76.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404605630i/10263483.jpg" alt=" photo d17d0161-dba0-4a06-8a82-857979689c76.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Melody Nicci Giovanni aka Mel/Boss/Bloody Melody is a 24 yr. old badass woman who was raised to rule the Italian Mafia, and be the 1st female boss. The Giovanni's are one of the most powerful families in Italy, and on the west coast.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/agungif.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404608769ra/10263777.gif" alt=" photo agungif.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Melody is the only child to mob boss Orlando Giovanni, and he trained her since the age of 7 to be fearless, ruthless, &amp; powerful. To show no mercy, and lead through fear. As a woman in the mob world, she was constantly having to prove herself to be treated as an equal.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/ddcf0e0d-db66-4be0-bbe3-9e1ec4b74d6f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404614994i/10264477.jpg" alt=" photo ddcf0e0d-db66-4be0-bbe3-9e1ec4b74d6f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Since Melody was young she has known she would one day wed their rivals son, Liam Alec Callahan aka Prince of Chicago. Liam was raised to one day head the Irish mob, and their mafia leading fathers arranged their marriage years ago, and signed a contract. Their marriage would put an end to the rivalry between the Irish &amp; the Italian, merge the two families, and end years of bloodshed. United they would also be extremely powerful!<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/81ffde03-1f9b-4bdb-b865-8590b71239a0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405048476i/10331750.jpg" alt=" photo 81ffde03-1f9b-4bdb-b865-8590b71239a0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The time has come for the wedding of Liam &amp; Melody, and Melody must move to Chicago to meet her fiancé, and start her new life. They were both born to rule. It's in their blood, &amp; is their calling. They live and breath drugs, money, &amp; murder, &amp; thrive off the constant battle for dominance. They are catholic, religious, and believe in being faithful. Power, respect, &amp; family are everything to them.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/64ef0ae3-bb0c-4cd2-b19e-4a3eae67a488.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404608922i/10263784.png" alt=" photo 64ef0ae3-bb0c-4cd2-b19e-4a3eae67a488.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Liam &amp; Melody finally meet. Liam has never even seen as much as a picture of Melody, but he is expecting a trophy wife he can control, that will be the perfect yes wife. He was taught that Irish men don't get true respect till they gain a wife by their side. He is ready to start this new chapter in his life.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/a7b71f7c-149d-4887-8009-f50498b62103.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405130824i/10348127.jpg" alt=" photo a7b71f7c-149d-4887-8009-f50498b62103.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Liam quickly learns the alliance between their families isn't going to go as smooth as he thought. He has met his match in Melody. They have rival bosses gunning for them, and must learn to work together as a team to survive. They are both willing to do anything to make their family proud, that's if they don't kill each other first. They have to learn to trust each other, and work as one.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/8099b52f-78a0-4b3b-b63c-361865e01d80.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404661966i/10269597.jpg" alt=" photo 8099b52f-78a0-4b3b-b63c-361865e01d80.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I thought this book was amazing! It is so different. I have never read a book where I was rooting for murderers, but believe it or not this couple is all about love &amp; family! Yes...shocking! ;)) This couple is sexy, ruthless, and badass! The sexual tension is on fire, and when these two finally decide to come together it is explosive! They are unstoppable! If you like lots of action, romance, &amp; can handle a bit of murder, then this book is for you. Can't wait for more in this series! :D <br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/01409679-427e-4fc5-8e13-555fdedf65f0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404660914i/10269511.jpg" alt=" photo 01409679-427e-4fc5-8e13-555fdedf65f0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-Orlando Giovanni's daughter was the key to every door.<br><br>-Swimming, shooting, sex, and speed were the only four things that could help clear my mind.<br><br>-He was known as the "Boogeyman of the East," and I was the unknown "Wicked Witch of the West."<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/84d6b0c8-c86f-409f-bda9-a3f7d2ea4d4e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404661593i/10269568.jpg" alt=" photo 84d6b0c8-c86f-409f-bda9-a3f7d2ea4d4e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-Liam, soon-to-be-fucking-dead, Callahan was walking down the stairs- my fucking stairs- with his sex hair high and his green eyes sharper than razor blades.<br><br>-I'm not now, nor shall I ever be, any man's arm candy."<br><br>-It is just business. Every last person we kill is for family. If we do not kill them, they kill us. It is the way of the world. It is self defense. It is survival.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/68c4ce10-3de2-4267-9aed-5491634dd556.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404661174i/10269534.jpg" alt=" photo 68c4ce10-3de2-4267-9aed-5491634dd556.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-Everyone is ruthless. They just don't know it. You do. I do. And that is why we are on top and will remain so."<br><br>-I was losing my mind, I could feel it, all I wanted to do was devour each and every fucking part of her.<br><br>-"You are mine, as I am yours.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/9958199a-b218-4853-bb5c-ee6fdb19e038.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405129964i/10347960.png" alt=" photo 9958199a-b218-4853-bb5c-ee6fdb19e038.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-My body cried out for his, and my mind both hated and loved that.<br><br>-My body now knew his touch and was accepting of it, in fact, it enjoyed it. I enjoyed it.<br><br>-How the fuck did she do it? How the fuck was she able to call forth hell and heaven in her eyes?<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/b7a9f486-3cb0-4fca-b045-acae13a598fe.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404935216i/10305198.jpg" alt=" photo b7a9f486-3cb0-4fca-b045-acae13a598fe.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-My family and loyalty start with you and you alone.<br><br>-I had no regrets for what I did. I didn't kill because I was a sick twisted motherfucker. Everything was for the betterment of the family.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/252ad606-2deb-4999-a215-5aaff2fe2009.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405131152i/10348191.jpg" alt=" photo 252ad606-2deb-4999-a215-5aaff2fe2009.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-"Murder is born of love, and love attains the greatest intensity in murder." ~Octave Mirbeau<br><br>-"My husband and I have never considered divorce. Murder sometimes, but never divorce." ~Joyce Brothers<br><br>-"He pulls a knife, you pull a gun, he sends one of yours to the hospital, you send one of his to the morgue..." ~Al Capone<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/a83b8a64-e34d-4dff-88ea-435c9aa05b66.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405546826i/10413241.jpg" alt=" photo a83b8a64-e34d-4dff-88ea-435c9aa05b66.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>LIVE on Amazon!!! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Ruthless-People-J-J-McAvoy-ebook/dp/B00LVA6QYM/ref=zg_bs_9536066011_1">http://www.amazon.com/Ruthless-People...</a></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('tzIV5luhUcj8s/4CtNmbJom2UoTbN8PGsa565lUHW9kiPSRp7hKlVU95oiy4L8IBAy18b+Blw26DKB4ysnTetw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GXk/eNh55UBsE6YG5DuW/PphXvH+krlqa4sdlbihj7aMdg73bcoR3d/Z+ijozc/bcPpwGsXAucJZDXlBX9IK2A==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText16135346011545811974" style="display:none">I’m a twenty-year-old something born in Montreal, Canada but currently living in Virginia for school. I would tell you want my major is however after two years I still have no idea what I’m doing.<br /><br />So I’m a writer (duh that’s how you found me), movie enthusiast, and self-proclaimed chef. I love music even though I can’t sing or dance to save my life. (That doesn’t necessarily stop me but you’ve been warned.)<br /><br />I started Ruthless People the summer of 2013 in hopes of giving myself a new type of love and crime drama. I never knew so many people thought like me! I feel truly blessed to have fans like you all!
